anusmarataḥ sā me hṛdayāt mā apasarpatu śrī bhagavān uvāca prahlādaḥ uvāca śastrāṇi pātitāni aṅge kṣiptaḥ yat ca agni saṃhatau anyāni ca api asādhūni yāni pitrā kṛtā ati me śrī bhagavān uvāca śrī bhagavān uvāca śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca tam pitā mūrdhni upāghrāya pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam prītimān ca abhavat tasmin anutāpī mahā asuraḥ guru pitroḥ cakāra evam śuśrūṣām saḥ api dharmatam pitari uparatim nīte narasiṃha svarūpiṇā viṣṇunā saḥ api daityānām maitreya abhūt patiḥ tatas tatas rājya dyutim prāpya karma śuddhi karīm kṣīṇa adhikāraḥ sa yadā puṇya pāpa vivirjitaḥ tadā sa bhagavat dhyānāt param nīrvāṇam āppavān śṛṇoti tasya pāpāni sadyas gacchanti saṃkṣayam ahorātra kṛtam pāpam prahlāda caritam naraḥ śṛṇvan paṭhan ca maitreya vyapohati na saṃśayaḥ paurmamāsyām amāvāsyām aṣṭamyām atha vā paṭhan dvādaśyām go pradāna phalam dvija prahlādam sakala āpatsu yathā rakṣitavān hariḥ tathā rakṣati yaḥ tasya śṛṇoti caritam sadā iti śrī viṣṇupurāṇe prathama iṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ prahlāda putraḥ āyuṣmān śibiḥ bāṣkalaḥ eva ca baleḥ putra śatam tu asīt bāṇa jyeṣṭham mahā mune hiraṇyākṣa sutāḥ ca āsan sarve eva mahā balā mahānābhaḥ mahābāhuḥ kālanābhaḥ tathā aparaḥ abhavan danu pūtrāḥ ca dvimūrdha śaṃbaraḥ tathā ayomukhaḥ śaṅkuśirāḥ kapilaḥ śaṅkaraḥ tathā ekacakraḥ mahābāhuḥ tārakaḥ ca mahā balaḥ ete danoḥ sutāḥ khyātāḥ vipracittiḥ ca viryavān svarbhānoḥ tu prabhā kanyā śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī upadānī hayaśiraḥ prakhyātāḥ vara kanyakāḥ vaiśvānara sute ca ubhe pulomā kālakā tathā tābhyā putra sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiḥ dānava sattamāḥ paulomāḥ kālake yāḥ ca mārīca tanayāḥ smṛtāḥ tatas apare mahā vīryāḥ dāruṇā stu ati nirghṛṇā tryaṃśaḥ śalyaḥ ca balavān nabhaḥ ca eva mahā balaḥ vātāpī namuciḥ ca eva ilvalaḥ khasṛmaḥ tathā svarbhānuḥ ca mahā vīryaḥ vaktra yodhī mahā asuraḥ ete vai dānavāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ danu vaṃśa vivardhanāḥ eteṣām putra pautraḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas samutpannāḥ su mahatā tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ ṣaḍ sutāḥ su mahā sattvāḥ tāmrāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ śukī śyenī ca bhāsī ca sugrīvī śuci gṛddhrakā śukī śukān ajanayat ulūka pratyulūkikān śyenī śyenān tathā bhāsī bhāsān gṛrdhyān ca gṛddhrī api śucyau dakān pakṣi gaṇān sugrīvī tu vyajāyata aśvān uṣṭrān gardabhān ca tāmrā vaṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ suparṇaḥ patatām śreṣṭhaḥ dāruṇaḥ pannagāśanaḥ surasāyām sahasram tu sarpāṇām amita ojasām aneka śirasām brahman khecarāmām mahātmanām suparṇa vaśā gāḥ brahman jajñire na eka mastakāḥ teṣām pradhāna bhūtāḥ tu śeṣa vāsuki takṣakāḥ śaṅkha śvetaḥ mahāpadmaḥ kambala aśvatarau tathā elā putraḥ tathā nāgaḥ karkoṭaka dhanañjayau ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ dandaśukāḥ viṣa ulbaṇāḥ gaṇam krodha vaśam viddhi tasyāḥ sarve ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ sthala jāḥ pakṣiṇā ubjāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ piśita aśanāḥ krodhāt tu piśācān ca janayāmāsa mahā balān gāḥ tu vai janayāmāsa surābhīḥ mahiṣīḥ tathā irā vṛkṣa latā vallīḥ tṛmajatīḥ ca sarvaśas svasā tu yakṣa rakṣāṃsi muniḥ apsarasaḥ tathā ārīṣṭā tu mahā sattvān gandharvān samajījanat ete kaśyapa dāyādāḥ kīrtitāḥ sthāṇu jaṅgamāḥ teṣām putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas gandharva bhogi devānām dānavānām ca sattama ditiḥ vinaṣṭa putrā vai toṣayāmāsa kāśyapam tayā ca ārādhitaḥ samyak kāśyapaḥ tapatām paraḥ samāhitā ati prayatā śaucinī dhārayiṣyasi iti eva suktvā tām devīm saṃgataḥ kaśyapaḥ muniḥ garbham ātma vadha arthāya jñātvā tam maghavān api śuśrūṣuḥ tām atha agacchat vinayāt amara adhipaḥ tasyāḥ ca eva antara prepsuḥ atiṣṭhat pākaśāsanaḥ ūne varṣa śate ca asyāḥ dadarśa antaram ātmanā a kṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucam ditiḥ śayanam āviśat nidrām ca āhārayāmāsa tasyāḥ kukṣim praviśya saḥ sampīḍyamānaḥ pajreṇa sa ruroda ādi dāruṇam mā rodīḥ iti tam śakraḥ punar punar abhāṣata ekaikam saptadhā cakre vajreṇa ari vidāriṇā devāḥ ekonapachcāśat sahāyāḥ vajrapāṇinaḥ iti śri viṣṇupurāme prathama aiṃśe ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca yadā abhiṣiktaḥ sa pṛthuḥ pūrvam rājye mahā ṛṣibhiḥ tatas krameṇa rājyāni dadau lokapitāmahaḥ nakṣatra graha viprāṇām vīrudhām ca api aśeṣatas somam rājye dadhat brahma yajñānām tapasām api rājñām vaiśravaṇam rājye jalānām varuṇam tathā ādityānām patim viṣṇum vasūnām atha pāvakam prajāpatīnām dakṣam tu vāsavam marutām api daityānām dānavānām ca prahlādam adhipam dadau pitṝṇām dharmarājānam yamam rājye abhyaṣecayat airāvatam patim dadau patatriṇām tu guruḍam devānām api vāsavam uccaiḥśravasam aśvānām vṛṣabham tu gavām api mṛgāṇām ca eva sarveṣām rājye siṃham dadau prabhuḥ śeṣam tu dandaśūkānām akarot patim avyayaḥ himālayam sthāvaraṇām munīnām kapilam munim nakhinām deṣṭriṇām ca eva mṛgāṇām vyāghram īśvaram vanaspatīnām rājāneḥ plakṣam ā eva abyaṣecayat evam eva anya jātīnām prādhānyena akarot prabhūn evam vibhajya rājyāni diśām pāla anantaram pūrvasyām diśi rājānam vairājasya prajāpateḥ diśāpālam sudhanvānam sutam vai saḥ abhyaṣecayat dakṣiṇasyām diśi tathā kardamasya prajāpateḥ putram śaṅkhapadam nāma rājānam saḥ abhyaṣecayat paścimasyām diśi tathā rajasaḥ putram acyutam ketumantam mahātmānam rājānam saḥ abhyaṣaicayat tathā hiraṇya romāṇam parjanyasya prajāpateḥ udīcyām diśi durdharṣam rājānam abhyaṣecayat taiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sa pattanā vibhūti bhūtāḥ rājānaḥ ye ca anye muni sattama ye bhaviṣyanti ye bhūtāḥ sarve bhūta īśvarāḥ dvija dānavānām ca ye nāthāḥ ye nāthāḥ piśitāśinām paśunām ye ca patayaḥ patayaḥ ye ca pakṣiṇām manuṣyāṇām ca sarpāṇām nāgānām adhipāḥ ca ye vṛkṣāṇām parvatānām ca grahāṇām ca api ye adhipāḥ atītāḥ vartamānāḥ ca ye bhaviṣyanti ca apare te sarve sarva bhūtasya viṣṇoḥ aṃśa samudbhāvāḥ sṛjati eṣa jagat sṛṣṭau sthitau pāti sanātanaḥ catur vibhāgaḥ saṃsṛṣṭau caturdhā saṃsthitaḥ sthitau marīci miśrāḥ patayaḥ prajānām ca anya bhāgaśas kālaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tasya aṃśaḥ sarva bhūtāni ca aparaḥ ittham caturdhā saṃsṛṣṭau vartate asau rajaḥ guṇaḥ eka aṃśena āsthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ karoti pratipālanam manu ādi rūpaḥ ca anyena kāla rūpaḥ ca sattvam guṇam samāśritya jagataḥ puruṣottamaḥ āśritya tamasaḥ vṛttimant akāle tathā punar kāla svarūpaḥ bhāgaḥ yaḥ sarva bhūtāni ca aparaḥ vibhūtayaḥ hareḥ etāḥ jagataḥ sṛṣṭi hetavaḥ viṣṇuḥ manu ādayaḥ kālaḥ sarva bhūtāni ca dvija rudraḥ kāla antaka ādyāḥ ca samastāḥ ca eva jantavaḥ caturdhā pralāyāya etāḥ janārdana vibhūtayaḥ jagat ādau tathā madhye sṛṣṭiḥ ā pralayā dvija brahma sṛjati ādi kāle marīci pramukhāḥ tatas kālena na vinā brahma sṛṣṭi niṣpādakaḥ dvija evam eṣa jagat straṣṭā jagat pātā tathā jagat sṛṣṭhi sthiti anta kāleṣu tridhā evam saṃpravartate guṇa pravṛtyā paramam padam tasya aguṇam mahat catuṣprakāram tat api svarūpam parama ātmanaḥ śrī maitreyaḥ uvāca mama ācakṣva yathānyāyam yat uktam paramam padam śrī parāsaraḥ uvāca maitreya kāraṇam proktam sādhanam sarva vastuṣu yoginaḥ mukti kāmasya prāṇāyāma ādi sādhanam sādhana ālambanam jñānam muktaye yoginām hi yat tad ālambana vijñānam dvitīyaḥ aṃśaḥ mahā mune nirvyāpāram anākhyeyam vyāpti mātram anūpamam ātma sambodha viṣayam sattā mātram alakṣaṇam praśāntam abhayam śuddham durvibhāvyam a saṃśrayam viṣṇoḥ jñāna mayasya uktam tat jñānam brahma saṃjñitam saṃsāra karṣaṇa uptau te yānti nirbīja tām dvijāḥ evaṃprakāram amalam nityam vyāpakam akṣayam kṣara akṣarā svarūpe te sarva bhūteṣu avasthite bahma viṣṇu śivāḥ brahman pradhānāḥ brahma śaktayaḥ tatas ca devāḥ maitreya nyūnāḥ dakṣa ādayaḥ tatas tatas manuṣyāḥ paśavau mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpāḥ nyūna anyūnatarāḥ ca eva vṛkṣa gulma ādayaḥ tathā sarva śakti mayaḥ viṣṇuḥ svarūpam brahmaṇaḥ param sa ālambanaḥ mahā yogaḥ sa bījaḥ yatra saṃsthitaḥ sa paraḥ para śaktīnām brahmaṇaḥ samanantaram kṣara akṣara mayaḥ viṣṇuḥ bibharti akhilam īśvaraḥ puruṣa avyākṛta mayam bhūṣaṇa astra svarūpavat śrī maitreyaḥ uvāca bhūṣaṇa astra svarūpa stham yat ca etat akhilam jagat śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca namaskṛtvā aprameyāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave kathayāmi yathā ākhyātam vasiṣṭhena bhavat bhūtādim indriya ādim ca dvidhā ahaṅkāram īśvaraḥ bibharti śaṃkha rūpeṇa śārṅga rūpeṇa ca sthitam pañca rūpā tu yā mālā vaijayantī gadābhṛtaḥ sā bhūta hetu saṃghātā bhūta mālā ca vai dvija yāni indriyāṇi aśeṣāṇi buddhi karma ātmakāni vai śara rūpāṇi aśeṣāṇi tāni dhatte janārdanaḥ bhūtāni ca hṛṣīkeśe manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca astra bhūṣaṇa saṃsthāna svarūpam rūpa varjitaḥ bibhārti māyā rūpā usau śreyase prāṇinām hariḥ sa vikāram pradhānam ca pumān ca eva akhilam jagat bibharti puṇḍahīkākṣaḥ tat evam parameśvaraḥ yā vidyā yā tathā avidyā yat sat yat ca asat avyayam kalā kāṣṭhā nimeṣa ādi dina ṛtu ayana hāyanaiḥ loka ātma mūrtiḥ sarveṣām pūrveṣām api pūrvajaḥ ādhāraḥ sarva vidyānām svayam eva hariḥ sthitaḥ deva mānuṣa paśu ādi śva rūpaiḥ bahubhiḥ sthitaḥ ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni tathā eva atharvāṇāni vai itihāsa upavedāḥ ca vedānteṣu tathā uktayaḥ vedāṅgāni samastāni manu ādi gaditāni ca śāstrāṇi aśeṣāṇi ākhyānāni anuvākāḥ ca ye kvacid kāvya ālāpāḥ ca ye kecid rītakāni akhilāni ca yāni mūrtāni amūrtāni yāni atra anyatra vā kvacid aham hariḥ sarvam idam janārdanaḥ na anyat tatas kāraṇa kārya jātam iti eṣa te aṃśaḥ prathamaḥ purāṇasya asya vai dvija kārttikyām puṣkara snāne dvādaśa abdena yat phalam bhavanti śṛṇvataḥ puṃsaḥ deva adya vara dāḥ mune iti śri viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe prathame aṃśe dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti śrī parāśara muni viracite śri viṣṇu para tva nirṇāyake śrīmati viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe prathama aṃśaḥ samāptaḥ atha śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe viṣṇu citti ātma prakāśa ākhya śrīdharīya vyākhyā dvaya upete dvitīyaḥ ūṃśaḥ prārabhyate śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥ yaḥ yam aṃśaḥ jagat sṛṣṭi sambandhaḥ gaditaḥ tvayā śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca mahā prajñāḥ mahā vīryāḥ vinītāḥ dayitāḥ pituḥ priyavrata sutāḥ khyātāḥ teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu āgnīdhraḥ ca agnibāhuḥ ca vapuṣmān dyutimān tathā jyotiṣmān daśamaḥ teṣām satyanāmā sutaḥ abhavat medha agnibāhu putrāḥ tu trayaḥ yoga parāyaṇāḥ jāti smārāḥ mahābhāgāna rājyāya manaḥ cakruḥ kriyām yathānyāyam aphalāka akṣiṇaḥ hi te priyavrataḥ dadau teṣām saptānām muni sattama jambūdvīpe mahābhāga sa ugnīdhrāya dadau pitā medhātitheḥ tathā prādāt plakṣadvīpam tathā aparam jyotiṣmantam kuśadvīpe rājānam kṛtāvān prabhuḥ dyutimantam ca rājānam krauñcadvīpe samādiśat śākadvīpa īśvaram ca api bhavyam cakre priyavrataḥ puṣkara adhipatim cakre savanam ca api sa prabhuḥ nābhiḥ kiṃpuruṣaḥ ca eva harivarṣaḥ ilāvṛtaḥ ramyaḥ hiraṇvān ṣaṣṭhaḥ ca kuru bhadrāśvaḥ eva ca ketumālaḥ tathā eva anyaḥ sādhu ceṣṭaḥ abhavan tṛpaḥ janbūdvīpa vi bhāgān ca teṣām vipra niśāmaya pitrā dattam himāhvam tu varṣam nābheḥ tu dakṣiṇam hemakūṭam tathā varṣam dadau kiṃpuruṣāya saḥ tṛtīyam naiṣadham varṣam harivarṣāya dattavān nīla acala āśritam varṣa ramyāya pradadau pitā śvetam yat uttaram tasmāt pitrā dattam hiraṇvate meroḥ purveṇa yat varṣa bhadrāśvāya pradattavān varṣeṣu eteṣu tān putrān abhiṣicya sa bhūmipaḥ sālāgrāmam mahā puṇyam maitreya tapase yayau kiṃpuruṣa ādi iti varṣā vyaṣṭau mahā mune teṣām svābhāviki siddhiḥ sukha prāyā hi ayatnataḥ na teṣu asti yuga avasthā kṣetreṣu aṣṭasu sarvadā himāhvayam tu vai varṣam nābeḥ āsīt mahātmanaḥ ṛṣabhāt bhārataḥ jajñe jyeṣṭhaḥ putra śatasya saḥ kṛtvā rājyam svadharmeṇa tathā eṣṭvā vividhān makhān abhiṣicya sutam vīram bharatam pṛthivīpatiḥ vānaprastha vidhānena tatra api kṛta niścayaḥ tapasā karṣita utyartham kṛśaḥ dhamani santataḥ nagnaḥ vīṭām mukhe kṛtvā vīrādhvānam tatas gataḥ tatas ca bhāratam varṣam etat lokeṣu gīyate bharatāya yatas pitrā dattam prātiṣṭhatā vanam kṛtvā samyak dadau tasmai rājyam iṣṭa makham pitā putra saṃkrāmita śrīḥ tu bharataḥ sa mahīpatiḥ yoga abhyāsa rataḥ prāṇān sālagrāme ayajat mune tasya putraḥ mahā vīryaḥ dhīmān tasmāt ajāyata tpaṣṭā tvaṣṭuḥ ca virajaḥ rajaḥ tasya api abhūt sutaḥ viṣvagjyoti pradhānāḥ te yaiḥ imāḥ vardhitāḥ prajāḥ taiḥ idam bhāratam varṣam nava bhedam alaṅkṛtam teṣām vaṃśa prasūtaiḥ ca bhuktā iyam bhāratī purā eṣa svāyaṃbhuvaḥ sargau yena idam pūritam jagat iti śrī viṣṇupurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī maitreyaḥ uvāca śrotum icchāmi aham tvattaḥ sakalam maṇḍalam bhuvaḥ yāvantaḥ sāgara dvīpāḥ tathā varṣāṇi parvatāḥ vanāni satitas puryaḥ deva ādīnām tathā mune yad pramāṇam idam sarvam yad ādhāram yad ātmakam śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca maitreya śrūyatām etat saṃkṣepāt gadataḥ mama na asya varṣa śatena api vaktum śakyaḥ hi vistaraḥ jambū plakṣa āhvayau dvīpau śālmaliḥ ca aparaḥ dvija kuśaḥ kraiñcaḥ tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraḥ ca eva saptamaḥ ete dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt dvātriṃśat mūrdhri vistṛta mūle ṣoḍaśa sāhasraḥ vistāraḥ tasya sarvaśas bhū padmasya asya śailaḥ asau karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ himāvān hemakūṭaḥ ca dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ lakṣa pramāṇaḥ dvau madhyau daśa hīnāḥ tathā apare bhāratam prathamam varṣam tatas kipuruṣam smṛtam uttarāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva yathā vai bhāratam tathā ilāvṛtam mahābhāga catvāraḥ ca atra parvatāḥ viṣkaṃbhā racitā meroḥ yojana ayutam ucchritaḥ navaiḥ sarobhiḥ ca samam dikṣu ete keśava acalāḥ purveṇa mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ viplalaḥ paścime pārśve mupārśvaḥ ca uttara smṛtaḥ ekādaśa śata āyāmāḥ pādapāḥ giri ketavaḥ jambūdvīpasya sā jambūḥ nāma hetuḥ mahā mune jambvāḥ tasyāḥ phalani vai patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvatas rasena teṣām prakhyātā tatra jāmbūnadī iti vai tad pānāt svaccham anāsāṃjanānām tatra jāyate tīra mṛd tad rasam prāpya sukha vāyu viśoṣitā jāmbūnada ākhyam bhavati suvarṇam siddha bhūṣaṇam bhadrāśvam pūrvatas meroḥ ketumālam ca paścime varṣe dve tu muni śreṣṭha tayoḥ madhyam ilāvṛtaḥ śītāmbhaḥ ca kumundaḥ ca kurarī mālyavān tathā vaikaṅka prasukhāḥ meroḥ pūrvatas kesara acalāḥ trikūṭaḥ śiśiraḥ ca eva pataṅgaḥ rucakaḥ tathā śikhivāsāḥ sa vaiḍūryaḥ kapilaḥ gandhamādanaḥ meroḥ anantara aṅgeṣu jaṭhara ādiṣu avasthitāḥ śaṃśakūṭaḥ utha ṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaḥ nāgaḥ tathā paraḥ kālañjana ādyāḥ ca tathā uttare kesara acalāḥ caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānām mahā purī tasyāḥ samantataḥ ca aṣṭau diśāsu vidiśāsu ca indra ādi lokapālānām prakhyātāḥ pravarāḥ puraḥ viṣṇu pāda viniṣkrāntā plāvayitvā indu maṇḍalam samantāt brahyaṇaḥ puryām gaṅga patati vai divaḥ sītā ca alakanandā ca cakṣuḥ bhadrā ca vai kramāt pūrveṇa śailāt śītā tu śailam yāti antarīkṣa gā tatas ca pūrva varṣaiṇa bhadrāśvā enā eti sa arṇavam prayāti sāgaram bhūtvā sapta bhedāḥ mahā mune paścima girīn atītya sakalān tatas paścimam ketumāla ākhya varṣam gatvā eti sāgaram bhadrā tathā uttara girīn uttarān ca tathā kurūn ā nīla niṣadha āyāmau mālyavat gandhamādanau tayoḥ madhya gataḥ merūḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ bhāratāḥ ketumālāḥ ca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravaḥ tathā patrāṇi loka padmasya maryādā śaila bāhyatas jaṭharaḥ hemakūṭaḥ ca maryādāparvatau ubhau tau dakṣima uttara āyāmau ā nīla niṣadha āyatau āśi iti yojana āyāmau arṇava anta vyavasthitau niṣadhaḥ pariyātraḥ ca maryādāparvatau ubhau pūrva paśca āyatau etau arṇava antar vyavasthitau jaṭhara ādyāḥ sthitāḥ meroḥ teṣām dvau dvau caturdiśam meroḥ caturdiśam ye tu proktāḥ kesaraparvatāḥ śīta anta ādyāḥ mune teṣām atīva hi manoramāḥ śailānām antare droṇyaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ su ramyāṇi tathā tāsu kānanāni purāṇi ca lakṣmī viṣṇu agni sūrya ādi devānām muni sattama tāsu āyatana varyāṇi juṣṭāni vara kinnaraiḥ gandharva yakṣa rakṣāṃsi tathā daiteya dānavāḥ krīḍanti tāsu ramyāsu śaila droṇīṣu aharnisam bhaumāḥ hi ete smṛtāḥ svargāḥ dharmiṇām ālayāḥ mune na etuṣu pāpa karmāṇaḥ yānti janma śataiḥ api bhadrāśve bhagavān viṣṇuḥ āste hayaśirāḥ dvija varājaḥ ketumāle tu bhārate kūrma rūpadhṛk matsya rūpaḥ ca govindaḥ kuruṣu āste janārdanaḥ kiṃpuruṣa ādini varṣāṇi aṣṭau mahā mune na teṣu śaukaḥ na āyāsaḥ na udvegaḥ kṣudh bhaya ādikam svasthāḥ prajāḥ nirātaṅkāḥ sarva duḥkha vivarjitāḥ daśa dvādaśa varṣāṇām sahasrāṇi sthira āyuṣaḥ na teṣu varṣate devaḥ bhaumāni ambhāṃsi teṣu vai kṛta tretā ādikam nā eva teṣu sthāneṣu kalpanā sarveṣu eteṣu varṣeṣu sapta sapta kula acalāḥ nadyaḥ ca śataśas tebhyaḥ prasūtāḥ yāḥ dvijottama iti śri viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca varṣam tat bhāratam nāma bhāratī yatra santatiḥ mahendraḥ malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimān ṛkṣa parvataḥ vindhyaḥ ca pārīyātraḥ ca sapta atra kulaparvatāḥ tiryaktvam narakam ca api yānti atas puruṣāḥ mune itas svargaḥ ca mokṣaḥ ca madhyam ca antaḥ ca gamyate bhāratasya asya varṣasya nava bhādān naśāmaya idradvīpaḥ kaseruḥ ca tāmraparṇām gabhastimān nāgadvīpaḥ tathā sāmyaḥ gandharvaḥ tu atha cāruṇaḥ ayam tu navamaḥ taṣām dvīpaḥ sa āgāra saṃvṛtaḥ yojanānām sahasram tu dvīpa ūyam dakṣiṇa uttarāt pūrve kirātāḥ yasya ante paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ madhye śabdrāḥ ca bhāgaśas śatadrū candrabhāgā ādyāḥ himayat pāda nirgatāḥ vedasmṛti mukha ādyāḥ ca pārīyātra udbhavāḥ mune narmadā murasā ādyāḥ ca nadyaḥ vindhya adri nirgatāḥ tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā prasūkhāḥ ṛkṣa saṃbhavāḥ godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇī ādikāḥ tathā sahya pāda udbhavāḥ nadyaḥ smṛtāḥ pāpa bhaya apahāḥ kṛtamālā tāmraparṇi prasukhāḥ malayodbhavāḥ trisāmā ca ṛṣikulyā ādyāḥ mahendra prabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ṛṣikulyā kumāra ādyāḥ śuktimat pāda sambhavāḥ āsām nadyaḥ upānadyaḥ santi anyāḥ ca sahasraśas tāsu ime kuru pāñcālāḥ madhyadeśa ādayaḥ janāḥ pūrva deśa ādikāḥ ca eva kāmarūpa nivāsinaḥ puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāḥ magadhāḥ dakṣiṇa ādyāḥ ca sarvaśas tathā aparāntāḥ saurāṣṭrāḥ śūra ābhīrāḥ tathā arbudāḥ kārūṣāḥ mālabāḥ ca eva pāriyātra nivāsinaḥ sauvīrāḥ saindhavāḥ hūṇāḥ sālvāḥ kosala vāsināḥ mādra ārāmāḥ tathā ambaṣṭhā pārasīka ādayaḥ tathā āsām pibanti salilam vasanti sahitāḥ sadā samīpatas mahābhāga hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākulāḥ kṛtam tretā dvāparan ca kaliḥ ca anyatra na kvacid dānāni ca atra dīyante para loka artham ādarāt yajñaiḥ yajña mayaḥ viṣṇuḥ anya dvīpeṣu ca anyathā atrā api bhāratam śreṣṭham janbūdvīpe mahā mune kadācid labhate jantuḥ mānuṣyam puṇya saṃcayāt gāyanti devāḥ kila gītakāni dhanyāḥ tu te bhārata bhūmi bhāge svarga apavarga āspada mārga bhūte bhavanti bhūyas puruṣāḥ sura tvāt karmāṇi a saṃkalpita tad phalāni saṃnyasya viṣṇo paramātma bhūte prāpsyāma dhanyāḥ khalu te manuṣyāḥ ye bhārate na indriya viprahīnāḥ lakṣa yojana vistāram saṃkṣepāt kathitam tava jambūdvīpam samāvṛtya lakṣa yojana vistaraḥ maitreya valaya ākāraḥ sthitaḥ kṣāra udadhiḥ bahis iti śri viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca kṣārodena yathā dvīpaḥ jambū saṃjñaḥ abhiveṣṭitaḥ saṃveṣṭya kṣāram udadhim plakṣadvīpaḥ tathā sthitaḥ jambūdvīpasya vistāraḥ śata sāhasra saṃmitaḥ saḥ evam dviguṇaḥ brahman plakṣadvīpaḥ udāhṛtaḥ sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpa īśvarasya vai jyeṣṭha śāntahayaḥ nāma śiśiraḥ tad anantaraḥ dhruvaḥ ca saptamaḥ teṣām plakṣadvīpa īśvarāḥ hi te pūrvam śāntahayam varṣam śiśiram ca sukham tathā maryādā kārakāḥ teṣām tathā anye varṣaparvatāḥ sapta eva teṣām nāmāni śṛṇuṣva muni sattama varṣa acaleṣu ramyeṣu varṣeṣu eteṣu ca anaghāḥ teṣu puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cirāt ca mriyate janaḥ teṣām nadyaḥ tu sapta eva varṣāṇām ca samudra gāḥ nāmataḥ tāḥ pravakṣyāmi śrutāḥ pāpam haranti yāḥ anutaptā śikhī ca eva vipāśā tridivāklamaḥ amṛtā sukṛtā ca eva saptā etāḥ tatra nimnagāḥ ete śailāḥ tathā nadyaḥ pradhānāḥ kathitāḥ tava tāḥ sadā hṛṣṭāḥ nadīḥ janapadāḥ tu te apasarpiṇī na teṣām vai na ca eva utsarpiṇī dvija plakṣadvīpa ādiṣu brahman śākadvīpa antikeṣu vai pañca varṣa sahasrāṇi janāḥ jīvanti anāmayāḥ dharmaḥ pañcasu atha eteṣu varṇa āśrama vibhāgaśaḥ āryakāḥ kurāraḥ ca eva vidiśyāḥ bhāvinaḥ ca te vipra kṣatri vaiśyāḥ te śūdrāḥ ca muni sattama jmabū vṛkṣa pramāṇaḥ tu tad madhye su mahān taruḥ sīmarūpi jagatstraṣṭā sarvaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ hariḥ plakṣadvīpa pramāṇena plakṣadvīpaḥ samāvṛtaḥ tathā eva ikṣuramodena pariveṣa anukāriṇā iti evam tava maitreya plakṣadvīpaḥ udāhṛtaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa mayā bhūyas śālmalam me nisāmaya śālma masya īśvaroḥ vīraḥ vapuṣmān tad sutān śṛṇu teṣām tu nāma saṃjñāni sapta varṣāṇi tāni vai vistāra dviguṇena atha sarvatas saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ tatra api parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyāḥ ratna yonayaḥ varṣa abhivyañjakāḥ ye tu tathā sapta ca nimnagāḥ kumudaḥ ced nataḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ ca balāhakaḥ ṣaṣṭhī mahiṣaḥ saptamaḥ tathā kakudmān parvata varaḥ sarit nāmāni me śṛṇu nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsām smṛtāḥ tāḥ pāpa śānti dāḥ śvetam ca haritam ca eva vaidyutam mānasam tathā jīmūtam rohitam ca eva suprabham ca api śobhanam sapta etāni tu varṣāṇi cāturvarṇya yutāni vai śālmale ye tu varṇāḥ ca vasanti ete mahā mune kapilāḥ ca aruṇāḥ pītāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ ca eva pṛthak pṛthak brahmaṇāḥ kṣatrayāḥ vaiśyāḥ śudrāḥ ca eva yajanti tam vāyu bhūtam makha śreṣṭhaiḥ yajvanaḥ yajña saṃsthitim śālmaliḥ su mahān vṛkṣaḥ nāmnā nirvṛti kārakaḥ eṣa dvīpaḥ samudreṇa su rodena samāvṛtaḥ surā udakaḥ parivṛtaḥ kuśadvīpena sarvatas jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe sapta putrān śṛṇuṣva tān udbhidaḥ veṇumān ca eva verathaḥ lambanaḥ dhṛtiḥ varṇāḥ tatra api catvāraḥ nija anuṣṭhāna tatparāḥ daminaḥ śuṣmiṇaḥ snehāḥ mandehāḥ ca mahā mune brahmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca anukrama uditāḥ vidrumaḥ hemaśailaḥ ca dyatimān puṣpavān tathā nadyaḥ ca sapta tāsām tu śṛṇu nāmāni anukramāt dhūtapāpā śivā ca eva pavitrā saṃmatiḥ tathā vidyudambhāḥ mahī ca anyā sarva pāpa harāḥ tu imāḥ anyāḥ sahasraśas tatra kṣudra nadyaḥ tathā acalāḥ kuśadvīpe guśa stambaḥ saṃjñayā tasya tat smṛtam tad pramāṇena sa dvīpaḥ ghṛtodena samāvṛtaḥ ghṛtodaḥ ca samudraḥ vai krauñcadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ krauñcadvīpaḥ mahābhāga śruyatām ca aparaḥ mahān tad nāmāni ca varṣāṇi teṣām cakre mahīpatiḥ kuśalaḥ mallagaḥ ca uṣṇaḥ pīvaraḥ thā andhakārakaḥ varṣa acalāḥ mahābuddhe teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu krauñcaḥ ca vāmanaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ ca andhakārakaḥ divāvṛt pañcamaḥ ca atra tathā anyaḥ puṇḍarīkavān dvīpa a dvīpeṣu ye śailāḥ yathā dvīpāni te tathā varṣeṣu eteṣu ramyeṣu tathā śaila vareṣu ca nivasanti nirātaṅkāḥ saha deva gaṇaiḥ prajāḥ puṣkarāḥ puṣkalāḥ dhanyāḥ titikhyāḥ ca mahā mune brahmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śudrāḥ ca anukrama uditāḥ nadīḥ maitreya te tatra yāḥ pibanti śṛṇuṣva tāḥ sapta pradhānāḥ śataśas tatra anyāḥ kṣudra nimnagāḥ kṣāntiḥ ca puṇḍarīkā ca saptā etāḥ varṣa nimnagāḥ tatra api viṣṇuḥ bhagavān puṣkāra ādyaiḥ jānārdanaḥ krauñcadvīpaḥ samudreṇa dadhimaṇḍa udakena ca āvṛtaḥ sarvatas krauñca dvīpa tulyena mānataḥ dadhimaṇḍa udakaḥ ca api śākadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ śākadvīpa īśvarasya api bhavyasya mu mahātmanaḥ sapta eva tanayāḥ taṣām dadau varṣāṇi sapta saḥ jaladaḥ ca kumāraḥ ca mukumāraḥ marīcakaḥ tad saṃjñāni eva tatra api sapta varṣāṇi anukramāt tatra api parvatāḥ spata varṣa viccheda kāriṇaḥ śākaḥ tatra mahā vṛkṣaḥ siddha gandharva sevitaḥ yatratya vāta saṃspārśāt āhlādaḥ jāyate paraḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cāturvarṇya samanvitāḥ nadyaḥ ca atra mahā puṇyāḥ sarva pāpa bhaya apahāḥ sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī dhenukā ca yā ikṣuḥ ca veṇukā ca eva gabhastī saptamī tathā anyāḥ ca śataśas tatra kṣudra nadyaḥ mahā mune mahīdharāḥ tathā santi śataśas utha sahasraśas tāḥ pibanti mudā yuktāḥ jalada ādiṣu ye sthitāḥ maryādā vyutkramaḥ na api teṣu deśeṣu saptasu vaṅgāḥ ca māgadhāḥ ca eva mānasāḥ mandagāḥ tathā vaṅgāḥ brahmaṇabhūyiṣṭhāḥ māgadhāḥ kṣatriyāḥ tathā vaiśyāḥ tu mānasāḥ teṣām śūdraḥ teṣām tu mandagāḥ śākadvīpe tu taiḥ viṣṇuḥ sūrya rūpa dharaḥ muneṃ śākadvīpaḥ tu maitreya kṣirodena samāvṛtaḥ śākadvīpa pramāṇena valayena iva veṣṭitaḥ kṣirā abdhiḥ sarvatas brahman puṣkara ākhyena veṣṭitaḥ dvīpena śākadvīpāt tu dvīguṇena samantataḥ mahāvīram tathā eva anya dhātukīkhaṇḍa saṃjñitam ekaḥ catra mahābhāga prakhyātaḥ varṣaparvataḥ mānāsottara saṃjñaḥ vai madhyatas valaya ākṛtiḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi ūrdhvam pañcāśat ucchritaḥ tāvat eva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvatas parimaṇḍalaḥ valaya ākāram ekaikam tayoḥ varṣam tathā giriḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ virāmayāḥ viśokāḥ ca rāga dveṣa ādi varjitāḥ na īrṣyā asūyā bhayam dveṣaḥ doṣaḥ lobha ādikaḥ na ca mahā pītam bahis varṣam dhātakīkhaṇḍam antatas satya anṛtena tatra āstām dvīpe puṣkara saṃjñite na tatra nadyaḥ śailāḥ vā dvīpe varṣa dvaya anvite tulya peṣāḥ tu manujāḥ devāḥ tatra eka rūpiṇaḥ varṇa āśrama ācāra hīnam dharma ācaraṇa varjitam trayī vārtā daṇḍanīti śuśrūṣā rahitam ca yat dhātakīkhaṇḍa saṃjñe atha mahāvīre ca vai mune svādu udakena udadhinā puṣkaraḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ samena puṣkarasya eva vistārāt maṇḍalam tathā evam dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ ca sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ nyūna atirikta tā teṣām kadācid nā eva jāyate anyūna anatiriktāḥ ca vardhanti āpaḥ hrasaṃti ca udaya astamaneṣu indoḥ pakṣayoḥ śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ daśa uttarāṇi pañca eva hi aṅgulānām śatāni vai apām vṛddhi kṣaṇaḥ dṛṣṭau sāmudrīṇām mahā mune ṣaṣ rasam bhuñjate vipra prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadā eva hi dviguṇā kāñcanī bhūmiḥ sarva jantu vivarjitā lokālokaḥ tatas śailaḥ jojana ayuta vistṛtaḥ ucchrāyeṇa api tāvanti sahasrāṇi acalaḥ hi saḥ tatas tamaḥ samāvṛtya tam śaulam sarvatas sthitam tamaḥ ca aṇḍa kaṭāhena samantāt pariveṣṭitam pañcaśat koṭi vistārā sā iyam urva mahā mune saha eva aṇḍa kaṭāhena sa dvīpa abdhi mahīdharā sā iyam dhātrī vidhātrī ca sarva bhūta guṇa adhikā ādhāra bhūtā sarveṣām maitreya jagatām iti iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca vistāraḥ eṣa kathitaḥ pṛthivyāḥ bhavataḥ mayā daśa sāhasram ekaikam pātālam muni sattama mahā ākhyam sutalam ca agryam pātālam ca api saptamam śukla a kṛṣṇa aruṇāḥ pītāḥ śarkarāḥ śaila kāñcanāḥ bhūmayaḥ yatra maitreya para grāsāt a maṇḍitāḥ teṣu dānava daiteyāḥ yakṣāḥ ca śataśas tathā svar lokāt api ramyāṇi pātālāni iti nāradaḥ āhlāda kāriṇaḥ śubhrāḥ maṇayaḥ yatra su prabhāḥ nāga ābharaṇa bhūṣāsu pātālam kena tat samam śaśi raśmiḥ na śītāya niśi dyotāya kevalam vanāni nadyaḥ ramyāṇi sarāṃsi kamala ākarāḥ puṃskokila abhilāpāḥ ca manojñāni ambarāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ati śubhrāṇi gandha āḍhyam ca anulepanam vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅgānām svanaiḥ a pūritāni ca etāni anyāni ca udāra bhagya bhogyāni tānavaiḥ pātālānām adhas ca āste viṣṇoḥ yā tāmasī tanuḥ śeṣa khyāḥ yat ruṇā anvaktum na śaktāḥ daitya dānavāḥ sa sahasra śirāḥ vyakta svasti kāmala bhūṣaṇaḥ phaṇāmaṇi sahasreṇa yaḥ sa vidyotayan diśaḥ kiriṭī sraj dharaḥ bhāti sa agniḥ śvetaḥ iva acalaḥ nīla vāsāḥ mada utsiktaḥ śveta hāra upaśobhitaḥ sa abhra gaṅgā pravāhaḥ usau kailāsa adriḥ iva aparaḥ upāsyate svayam kāntyā yaḥ vāruṇyā ca mūrtayā saṃkarṣaṇa ātmakaḥ rūdraḥ niṣkramya atti jagattrayam sa bibhrat śekharībhūtam aśeṣam kṣiti maṇḍalam āste pātāla mūla sthaḥ śeṣaḥ aśeṣa sura arcitaḥ tasya vīryam prabhāvaḥ ca svarūpam rūpam eva ca na hi varṇayitum śakyam jñātum ca tridaśaiḥ api yasya eṣā sakalā pṛthvī phaṇāmaṇi śikhā rūṇā yadā vijṛmbhat enantaḥ mada āghūrṇita locanaḥ tadā calati bhūḥ eṣā sa abdhi toyā sa kānanā gandharva apsarasaḥ siddhāḥ kinnara uraga cāraṇāḥ na antam guṇānām gacchanti tena anantaḥ yam avyayaḥ muhur śvāsa anila apāstam yāti diś kṣoda vāsatām yam ārādhya pūrāṇa ṛṣiḥ gargaḥ jyotīṃṣi tattvataḥ tena iyam nāga varyeṇa śirasā vidhṛtā mahī bibharti mālām lokānām sa deva asura mānuṣām iti śrī viṣṇu mahāhurāṇe dvitīraye aṃśe pañcamaḥ adhyāya parāśaraḥ uvāca pāpinaḥ yeṣu pātyante tān śṛṇuṣva mahā mune asipatravanam kṛṣṇaḥ lālābhakṣaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ tathā pūya vahaḥ pāpaḥ vahni jvālaḥ hi adhas sirāḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ kālasūtraḥ ca tamaḥ ca avīciḥ eva ca śvabhojanaḥ utha apratiṣṭhaḥ ca apraciḥ ca tathā paraḥ iti evamādayaḥ ca anye narakāḥ bhṛśa dārūṇāḥ yamasya viṣaye ghorāḥ śastra agni bhaya dāyinaḥ patanti yeṣu puruṣāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ tu ye kūṭa sākṣī tathā asamyak pakṣapātena yaḥ vadet hanti rāja bhaṭān ca yaḥ sādhvī vikraya kṛt bandha pālaḥ kesari vikrayī snuṣām sutām ca api gatvā mahājvāle nipātyate avamantā gurūṇām yaḥ yaḥ ca ākroṣṭā nara adhamaḥ veda dūṣayitā ayaḥ ca veda vikrayakaḥ ca yaḥ agamya gāmī yaḥ ca syāt te yānti lavaṇam dvija deva dvija pitṛ dveṣṭā ratna dvaṣayitā ca yaḥ pitṛ deva atithīn tyaktvā paryaśnāti nara adhamaḥ karoti yaḥ ca yaḥ ca khaṅga ādi kṛt naraḥ a yājya yājakaḥ ca eva tathā nakṣatrasūcakaḥ vegī pūyavahe ca ekaḥ yāti maṣṭa anna bhuṅgaraḥ lākṣā māsa rasānām ca tilānām lavaṇasya ca mārjāra kukkuṭa chāga śva varāha vihaṅgamān raṅga upajīvī kaivartaḥ kumḍāśī garadaḥ tathā sūcī māhiṣakaḥ ca eva parva kārī ca yaḥ dvijaḥ agāra dāhī mitra ghnaḥ śākuniḥ grama yājakaḥ makha hā grāma hantā ca yāti vaitaraṇīm naraḥ retaḥ pāta ādi kartāraḥ maryādā bhedinaḥ hi ye te kṛṣṇe yānti aśaucāḥ ca kuhaka ājīvinaḥ ca ye vratānām lopakaḥ yaḥ ca sva āśramāt vicyutaḥ ca yaḥ ete ca anye ca narakāḥ śataśas utha sahasraśas yeṣu duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ pacyante yātanā gatāḥ yathā eva pāpāni etāni tathā anyāni sahasraśas karmaṇā manasā vācā nirayeṣu patanti te adhas śirobhiḥ dṛśyante nārakaiḥ divi devatāḥ devāḥ ca adhomukhān sarvān adhas paśyanti nārakān sthāvarāḥ krimayaḥ ubjāḥ ca pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaḥ narāḥ dhārmikāḥ tridaśāḥ tad hat mokṣiṇaḥ ca yathākramam sahasra bhāga prathamāḥ dvitīya anukramāḥ tathā sarve hi ete mahābhāgāḥ yāvat mukti samāśrayāḥ pāpa kṛt yāti narakam prāyās citta parāṅmukhaḥ pāpānām anurūpāṇi prāyaścittāni yat yathā pāpe gurūṇi guruṇi su alpāni alpe ca tad vidaḥ prāyaścittāni maitreya jaguḥ svāyaṃbhuva ādayaḥ prāyaścittāni aśeṣāṇi tapaḥ karma tmakāni vai yāni kṛṣṇa anusmaraṇam param kṛte pāpe anutāpaḥ vai yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate prāyaścittam tu tasya ekam hari saṃsmaraṇam param prātar niśi tathā sandhyā madhyāhna ādiṣu saṃsmaran nārāyaṇam avāpnoti sadyas pāpa kṣayan naraḥ viṣṇu saṃsmaraṇāt kṣīṇa samasta kleśa sañcayaḥ kva nāka pṛṣṭha gamanam punarāvṛtti lakṣaṇam tasmāt aharniśam viṣṇu saṃsmaran puruṣaḥ mune na yāti narakam martyaḥ saṃkṣīṇa akhila pātakaḥ vastu ekam eva duḥkhāya sukhāya iṣrī āgamāya ca tat eva prītaye bhūtvā jāyate tasmāt duḥkha ātmakam nā asti na ca kiñcid sukha ātmakam manasaḥ sukha duḥkha ādi lakṣamaḥ jñānam eva param brahma jñānam bandhāya ca iṣyate jñāna tmakam idam viśvam na jñānāt vidyate param evam etat mayā ākhyātam bhavataḥ maṇḍalam bhuvaḥ pātālāni ca sarvāṇi narakāḥ dvija samudrāḥ parvatāḥ ca eva dvīpāḥ varṣāṇi nimnagāḥ saṃkṣepāt sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhuvarloka ādikān lokān śrotum icchāmi aham mune tathā eva graha saṃsthānam pramāṇāni yathā tathā śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca sa samudra sarit śailā tāvatī pṛthivī smṛtā yāvat pramāṇā pṛthivī vistāra parimaṇḍalāt nabhaḥ tāvat pramāṇam vai vyāsa maṇḍalataḥ dvija lakṣāt divākarasya api maṇḍalam śaśinaḥ sthitam śata sahasre tu yojanānām niśākarāt nakṣatra maṇḍalam kṛtstram upariṣṭāt prakāśate tāvat pramāṇa bhāge tu budhasya api uśanāḥ sthitaḥ saptarṣi maṇḍalam tasmāt lakṣam ekam dvijottamā ṛṣibhyaḥ tu sahasrāṇām śatāt ūrdhvam vyavasthitaḥ ijyā phalasya bhūḥ eṣā ijyā ca atra pratiṣṭhitā dve koṭī tu janaḥ lokaḥ yatra te brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ vairājāḥ yatra te devāḥ sthitāḥ dāha vivarjitāḥ pātālāni ca sapta eva brahmāṇḍasya eṣa vistaraḥ daśa uttareṇa payasā maitreya aṇḍam ca tat vṛtam vahniḥ ca vāyunā vāyuḥ maitreya nabhasā vṛtaḥ bhūtādinā nabhaḥ saḥ api mahatā pariveṣṭitaḥ deśa uttarāmi aśeṣāṇi maitreya etāni sapta vai tat anantam asaṃkhyāta pramāṇam ca api vai yatas hetu bhūtam aśeṣasya prakṛtiḥ sā parā mune aṇḍānām tu sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca īdṛśānām tathā tatra koṭi koṭi śatāni ca pradhānam ca pumān ca eva sarva bhūta ātma bhūtayā viṣṇu śaktyā mahābuddhe vṛtau saṃśraya dharmiṇau tayoḥ sā eva pṛthak bhāva kāraṇam saṃśrayasya ca kṣobha kāraṇa bhūtā ca sarga kāle mahāmate yathā saktam jale vātaḥ bibharti kaṇikā śatam śaktiḥ sā api tathā viṣṇoḥ pradhāna puruṣa ātmakam yathā ca pāda yauḥ mūla skandha śākhā ādi saṃyutaḥ ādi bījāt prabhavati bījāni anyāni vai tatas te api tad lakṣaṇa dravya kāraṇa anugatāḥ mune evam avyākṛtāt pūrvam jāyante mahat ādayaḥ viśaṃṣā antāḥ statas tebhyaḥ saṃbhavanti asura ādayaḥ tebhyaḥ ca putrāḥ teṣām ca putrāṇām apare sutāḥ bījāt vṛkṣa praroheṇa yathā na apacayaḥ taroḥ bhūtānām bhūta sargeṇa na eva asti apacayaḥ tathā sannidhānāt yathā ākāśa kāla ādyāḥ kāraṇam taroḥ vrīhi bīje yathā mūlam nālam patra aṅkurau tathā kāṇḍakoṣaḥ tu puṣpam ca kṣīram tadvat ca taṇjulāḥ tuṣāḥ kaṇāḥ ca santaḥ vai yānti āvirbhāvam ātmanaḥ tathā karmasu anekeṣu deva ādyāḥ samavasthitāḥ viṣṇuśaktim samāsādya praroham upayānti vai iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ prāśaraḥ uvāca vyākhyātam ā etat brahmaṇḍa saṃsthānam tava suvrata tatas pramāṇa saṃsthāne sūrya ādīnām śṛṇuṣva mai yojanānām sahasrāṇi bhāskarasya rathaḥ nava īṣā daṇḍaḥ tathā eva asya dviguṇaḥ muni sattama yojanānām tu tasya akṣaḥ tatra cakram pratiṣṭhitam tri nābhimati pañca are hayāḥ ca sapta chadāṃsi teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu gāyatrī ca bṛhatī uṣṇih jagatī triṣṭubhā iva ca anuṣṭubh paṅktiḥ iti uktā chandāṃsi harayaḥ raveḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi dvitīyaḥ akṣaḥ vivasvataḥ ā akṣa pramāṇam ubhayoḥ pramāṇam tat yuga ardhayoḥ mānasottara śailasya pūrvatas vāsavī purī dakṣiṇe tu varuṇasya ca uttareṇa ca somasya tāsām nāmāni me śṛṇu vasvaukasārā śakrasya yāmyā saṃyamanī tathā kāṣṭhām gataḥ dakṣiṇatas kṣipta iṣuḥ iva sarpati maitreya bhagavān bhānuḥ jyotiṣām cakra saṃyutaḥ ahar rātra vyavasthāna kāraṇam bhagavān raviḥ deva yānaḥ paraḥ panthāḥ yoginām kleśa saṃkṣaye vidiśāsu tu aśeṣāsu tathā brahman diśāsu ca yaiḥ yatra dṛśyate bhāsvān sa teṣām udayaḥ smṛtaḥ udaya astamana ākhyam hi darśana adarśanam raveḥ śakra ādīnām pure tiṣṭhan spṛśati eṣa puratrayam uditaḥ vardhamāna abhirāma adhyāhnāt tapan raviḥ udaya astamanābhyām ca smṛte pūrva apare diśau yāvat purastāt tapati tāvat pṛṣṭhe ca pārśvayoḥ tasmāt diśi uttarasyām vai divā rātriḥ sadā eva hi sarveṣām dvīpa varṣāṇām seruḥ uttaratas yatas vahnoḥ prabhā tathā bhānuḥ dineṣu āviśati dvija atīva vahni saṃyogāt atas sūryaḥ prakāśate tejasī bhāskara āgneye prakāśa uṣṇa svarūpiṇī paraspara anupraveśāt āpyāyete divāniśam ā ahar rātram viśati ambhaḥ tamaḥ prākāśya śīlavat ātāmrāḥ hi bhavati āpaḥ divā nakta praveśanāt dinam viśati ca eva aṃbhaḥ bhāskareḥ tam upeyuṣi evam puṣkara madhyena yadā yāti divākaraḥ triṃśat bhāgaḥ tu medinyāḥ tadā mauhūrtikī gatiḥ karoti ahar tathā rātrim vimuñcan medinīm dvijaḥ tatas kumbham ca mīnam ca rāśeḥ rāśi antaram dvija tatas ca mithunasya ante parām kāṣṭhām upāgataḥ rāśim karkaṭakam prāpya kurute dakṣiṇāyanam dakṣiṇa prakrame sūryaḥ tathā śīghram pravartate tasmāt prakaṣṭām bhūmim tu kālena alpena gacchati sūryaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ śaighryāt muhūrte dakṣiṇāyane trayodaśa ardham ṛkṣāṇām ahnā tu carati dvija muhūrtaiḥ tāvat ṛkṣāṇi naktam aṣṭādaśaiḥ caran tasmāt dīrgheṇa kālena bhūmim alpām tu gaccati aṣṭādaśa suhūrtam yat uttarāyaṇa paścimam trayodaśa ardham ahnā tu ṛkṣāṇām carate raviḥ muhūrtaiḥ tāvat ṛkṣāṇi rātrau dvādaśabhiḥ caran ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ madhye bhramataḥ maṇḍalāni tu divā naktam ca sūryasya mandā śīghrā ca vai gatiḥ manda ahni yasmin nayane śīghrā naktam tadā gatiḥ śīghrā niśi yadā ca asya tadā mandā divā gatiḥ eka pramāṇam eva eṣa mārgam yāti divākaraḥ ahorātreṇa yaḥ bhuṅkte samastāḥ rāśayaḥ dvija ṣaṭ eva rāśīn yaḥ bhuṅkte rātrau anyān ca ṣaṭ divā rāśi pramāṇa janitā dīrgha hrasva ātma tā dine tathā niśāyām rāśīnām pramāṇaiḥ laghu dīrgha tā uṣāḥ rātriḥ samākhyātā a vyuṣṭiḥ ca api ucyate dinam procyate ca tathā saṃdhyā uṣā vyuṣṭyoḥ yat antaram saṃdhyā kāle ca saṃprāpte raudre parama dāruṇe mandehāḥ rākṣasāḥ ghorāḥ sūryam icchinti khāditum prajāpati kṛtaḥ śāpaḥ teṣām maitreya rakṣasām akṣaya tvam śarīrāṇām maraṇam ca dine dine oṅkāra brahma saṃyuktam gāyatryā ca abhimantritam tena dahyanti te pāpāḥ vajrībhūtena vāriṇā sūryojyotiḥ sahasra aṃśu samāḥ dīpyati bhāskaraḥ oṅkāraḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ tridhāmā vacasām patiḥ tad uccāraṇataḥ te tu vināśam yānti rākṣasāḥ paraḥ sūryaḥ yaḥ ntar jyotiḥ a saṃplavam tena saṃpreritam jyotiḥ oṃkāreṇa atha dīptimat dahati aśeṣa rakṣāṃsi mandeha ākhyāni aghāni vai tasmāt na ullaṅghanam kāryam saṃdhyā upāsana karmaṇaḥ sa hanti sūryam sandhyāyāḥ na upāstim kurute tu yaḥ tatas prayāti bhagavān brāhmaṇaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ kāṣṭhāḥ nimeṣāḥ daśa pañca ca eva triṃśat ca kāṣṭhāḥ gaṇayet kalām ca hrāsa vṛddhī tu aharbhāgoḥ divasānām yathākramam sandhyā muhūrta mātrā vai hrāsa vṛddhau samā smṛtā prātar smṛtaḥ tatas kālaḥ bhāgaḥ ca ahnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ tasmāt prātastanāt kālāt tra muhūrtaḥ tu saṅgavaḥ tasmāt mādhyāhnikāt kālāt aparāhnaḥ iti smṛtaḥ trayaḥ eva muhūrtāḥ tu kālabhāgaḥ smṛtaḥ budhaiḥ ā aparāhne vyatīte tu kālaḥ sāyāhnaḥ eva ca daśa pañca muhūrtam vai ahar vaiṣuvatam smṛtam karkaṭa avasthite bhānau dakṣiṇāyanam ucyate triṃśat muhūrtam kathitam ahorātram tu yat mayā māsaḥ pakṣa dvayena uktaḥ dvau māsau ca arka jau ṛtuḥ ṛtu trayam ca api ayanam dve ayane varṣa saṃjñite saṃvatsara ādayaḥ pañca catur māsa vikalpitāḥ vatsaraḥ pañcamaḥ ca atra kālaḥ yam yuga saṃjñitaḥ yaḥ śvetasya uttaraḥ śailaḥ śṛṅgavān iti viśrutaḥ trīṇi tasya tu śṛṅgāṇi mairayam śṛṅgavān smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇam ca uttaram ca eva madhyam vaiṣuvatam tathā prathame kṛttikā bhāge yadā bhāsvān tadā śaśī viśākhānām caturthe aṃśe mune tiṣṭhati asaṃśayam viśākhānām yadā sūryaḥ carati aṃśam tṛtīyakam tadā candram vijānīyāt kṛttikā śirasi sthitam tadā eva viṣuva ākhyaḥ ayam kālaḥ puṇyaḥ abhidhīyate tadā dāna ādi deyāni devebhyaḥ prayata ātmabhiḥ ahorātra ardha māsā tu kalāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kṣaṇāḥ tathā paurṇamāsī tathā jñeyā amāvāsyā tathā eva ca sinīvālī kuhūḥ ca eva ekā ca anumatiḥ tathā lokāḥ lokaḥ ca yaḥ śailaḥ prāk uktaḥ bhavataḥ mayā lokapālāḥ tu catvāraḥ tatra tiṣṭhanti suvratāḥ nirdhandvāḥ nirabhīmānāḥ nistandrāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ uttaram pad agastyasya ajavīthyāḥ ca dakṣiṇam pitṛyānaḥ sa vai panthāḥ vaiśvānara pathāt bāhis tatra āsate mahātmānaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ye agnihotriṇaḥ bhūta āraṃbha kṛtam brahma śaṃsantaḥ ṛtvij udyatāḥ prārabhante tu ye lokāḥ teṣām panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ jāyamānāḥ tu pūrve ca paścimānām gṛheṣu vai paścimāḥ ca eva pūrveṣām jāyante vidhaneṣu iha evam āvartamānāḥ te tiṣṭhanti niyata vratāḥ savituḥ dakṣiṇam mārgam śritāḥ hi a candra tārakam nāgāvīthī uttaram yat ca saptarṣibhyaḥ ca dakṣiṇam uttaraḥ savituḥ panthāḥ deva yānaḥ ca sa smṛtaḥ tatra te vāsinaḥ siddhāḥ vimalāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhvaretaḥ sām icchā dveṣa apravṛttyā ca bhūta ārambha vi varjanāt punar ca kāma asaṃyogāt śabda ādeḥ deṣa darśanāt iti ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhāḥ te mṛta tvam hi bhejire ābhūtasaṃplavam sthānam amṛta tvam vibhāvyate brahmahatyā aśvamedhābhyām pāpa puṇya kṛtaḥ vidhiḥ kṣayam āyāti tāvat tu bhūmeḥ ā bhūta saṃplavāt etat viṣṇu padam divyam tṛtīyam vyomni bhāsuram nirdhūta doṣa paṅkānām yatīnām saṃyata ātmanām apuṇya puṇya uparame kṣīṇa aśeṣa āpti hetavaḥ dharma dhruva ādyāḥ tiṣṭhanti yatra te lokasākṣiṇaḥ divi iva cakṣuḥ ātatam yoginām tad maya ātmanām viveka jñāna dṛṣṭam ca tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam yasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ bhāsvān meḍhī bhūtaḥ svayam dhruvaḥ megheṣu saṃgatā vṛṣṭiḥ vṛṣṭeḥ sṛṣṭeḥ ca poṣaṇam āpyāyanam ca sarveṣām deva ādīnām mahā mune tatas ca ājya āhuti dvārā poṣitāḥ te havirbhujaḥ vṛṣṭeḥ kāraṇa tām yānti bhūtānām sthitaye punar evam etat padam viṣṇoḥ tṛtīyam amala ātmakam ādhāra bhūtam lokānām trayāṇām vṛṣṭi kāraṇam gaṅgā deva aṅganā aṅgānām anulepana piñjarā vāma pāda ambuja aṅguṣṭha nakha strotaḥ vinirgatām viṣṇoḥ bibhārti yām bhaktyā śirasā aharniśam dhruvaḥ tatas saptarṣayaḥ yasyāḥ prāṇāyāma parāḥ tiṣṭhanti vīci mālābhiḥ uhyamāna jaṭā jale vāri oghaiḥ saṃtataiḥ yasyāḥ plāvitam śaśi maṇḍalam meru pṛṣṭe patati uccais niṣkrāntā śaśi maṇḍalāt sītī ca alakanandā ca cakṣurbhadrā ca saṃsthitā bhedam ca alakanandā ākhyam yasyāḥ śarvaḥ api dakṣiṇām dadhāra śirasā prītya varṣāṇām adhikam śatam śambhoḥ jaṭā kalāpāt ca viniṣkrāntāḥ aśthi śarkarāḥ plāvayitvā divam ninye yā pāpān sagara ātmajān strātasya salile yasyāḥ sadyas pāpam praṇaśyati dattāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ yatra apaḥ tanayaiḥ śraddhayā anvitaiḥ yasyām iṣṭvā mahā yajñaiḥ yajñeśam puruṣottamam snānāt vidhūta pāpāḥ ca yad jalaiḥ yatayaḥ tathā prāptāḥ nirvāṇam uttamam śrutā abhilaṣitā dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā pītā avagāhitā yā pāvayati bhūtāni kīrtitā ca divedine gagāgaṅgā iti yaiḥ nāma yojanānā śataṣu api yatas sā pāvanāya alam trayāṇām jagatām api iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī pāraśaraḥ uvāca tārā mayam bhagavataḥ śiśumāra ākṛti prabhoḥ sūryācandramasau tārā grahaiḥ saha śiśumāra ākṛti proktam yat rūpam jyotiṣām divi nārāyaṇaḥ ayanam dhāmnām tasya ādhāraḥ svayam hṛdi sa tārā śiśumārasya dhruvaḥ pucche vyavasthitaḥ ādhāraḥ śiśumārasya sarva adhyakṣaḥ janārdanaḥ tad ādhāram jagat ca idam sa deva asura mānuṣam yena vipra vidhānena tat mama ekamanāḥ śṛṇu vivasvān aṣṭabhiḥ māsaiḥ ādāya apaḥ rasa ātmikāḥ vivasvān aṃśubhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ādāya jagataḥ jatam somam puṣmā ati atha induḥ ca vāyu nāḍī mayaiḥ divi nālaiḥ vikṣipate abhreṣu dhūma agni anila mūrtiṣu abhra sthāḥ prapatanti āpaḥ vāyunā samudīritāḥ saṃskāram kāṃla janitam maitreya āsādya nirmalāḥ sarit samudra bhomāḥ tu tathā āpaḥ prāṇi sambhavāḥ catuṣprakārā bhagavān ādatte savitā mune ākāśagaṅgā salilam tathā ādāya gabhastimān dṛṣṭa sūryam hi yat vāri patati abhraiḥ vinā divaḥ ākāśagaṅgā salilam tat gobhiḥ kṣipyate raveḥ kṛttikā ādiṣu ṛkṣeṣu viṣameṣu ca yat divaḥ dṛṣṭa arka patitam jñeyam tat gāṅgam diggaja ujjhitam ubhayam puṇyam atyartham nṛṇām pāpa bhaya apaham ākāśagaṅgā salilam divyam snānam mahā mune yat tu maighaiḥ samutsṛṣṭam vāri tat prāṇinām dvija puṣṇāti auṣadhayaḥ sarvāḥ jīvanāya amṛtam hi tat tena vṛddhim parām nītaḥ sakalaḥ ca oṣadhī gaṇaḥ sādhakaḥ phala pākantaḥ prajānām dvija jāyate tena yajñān yathā proktān mānavāḥ śāstra cakṣuṣaḥ evam yajñāḥ ca vedāḥ ca varṇāḥ ca dvija pūrvakāḥ sarve deva nikāyāḥ ca sarve bhūta gaṇāḥ ca ye vṛṣṭyā dhṛtam idam sarvam annam niṣpādyate yayā sā api niṣpādyate vṛṣṭiḥ savitrā muni sattama dhruvasya śiśupāraḥ asau saḥ api nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ tasya saṃsthitaḥ bibhartā sarva bhūtānām ādi bhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca tryaśīti maṇḍala śatam kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram dvayoḥ ārohaṇa avarohābhyām bhānoḥ abdena yā gatiḥ maitreya syandane bhānoḥ sapta māsa adhikāriṇaḥ aryamā pulahaḥ ca eva rathaujāḥ puñcikasthalā varuṇaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ rambhā ca sahajanyā huhūrathaḥ rathacitraḥ tathā śukre vasanti āṣāḍha saṃjñake indraḥ viśvāvasuḥ srotāḥ elā putraḥ tathā aṅgirāḥ vivasvān ugrasenaḥ ca bhṛguḥ āpūraṇaḥ tathā anumlocā śaṅkhapālaḥ vyāghraḥ bhādrapade tathā pūṣā ca suruciḥ vātaḥ gautamaḥ utha dhanañjayaḥ suṣeṇaḥ anyaḥ ghṛtācī ca vasanti āśvayuje ravau aṃśaḥ kāśyapa tārkṣyāḥ tu mahāpadmaḥ tathā urvaśī citrasenaḥ tathā vidyut mārgaśīrṣa idhi kāriṇaḥ kratuḥ bhagaḥ tatas ūrṇāyuḥ sphūrjaḥ kārkoṭakaḥ tathā ariṣṭanemiḥ ca eva anyā pūrvācittiḥ vara apsarāḥ loka prakāśana arthāya vigra varya adhikāriṇaḥ śrūyatām ca apare sūrye viṣṇuḥ aśvataraḥ rambhā sūryavarcāḥ ca satyajit savituḥ maṇḍale brahman viṣṇu sakti upabṛṃhitāḥ nṛtyanti apsarasaḥ yānti sūryasya anu niśācarāḥ vahanti pannagāḥ yakṣaiḥ kriyate abhīṣu saṃgrahaḥ saḥ ayam sapta gaṇaḥ sūrya maṇḍale muni sattama hima uṣṇa vāri vṛṣṭīnām hetuḥ sva samayam gataḥ iti kṣiviṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ maṇḍale hima tāpa ādeḥ kāraṇam tat mayā śrutam vyāpāraḥ ca api kathitaḥ gandharva uraga rakṣasām ṛṣīṇām vālakhilyānām tathā eva apsarasām guro yakṣāṇām ca rathe bhānoḥ viṣṇu śakti dhṛta ātmanām yadi sapta gaṇaḥ vāri himam uṣṇam ca varṣati tat kim atra raveḥ yena vṛṣṭiḥ sūryāt iti īryate parāśaraḥ uvāca yathā sapta gaṇaḥ api ekaḥ prādhānyena adhikaḥ raviḥ sarva śaktiḥ parā viṣṇo ṛk yajuḥ sāma saṃjñitā sa eṣa viṣṇuḥ sthitaḥ sthityām jagataḥ pālana udyataḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma bhūtaḥ ūntaḥ savituḥ dvijatiṣṭhati trayī mayī viṣṇuśaktiḥ avasthānam karoti vai ṛcaḥ stuvantiḥ pūrvāhne madhyāhne tha yajūṃṣi vai bṛhat rathantara ādīni sāmāni ahnaḥ kṣaye ravim aṅgam eṣā trayī viṣṇo ṛk yajuḥ sāma saṃjñitā viṣṇuśaktiḥ avasthānam sadā āditye karoti sā na kevalam raveḥ śaktiḥ vaiṣṇavī sā trayī mayī sarga ādau ṛk mayaḥ brahmā sthitau viṣṇuḥ yajuḥ mayaḥ rudraḥ sāma mayaḥ antāya tasmāt tasya aśuciḥ thvaniḥ evam sā sāttvikī śaktiḥ vaiṣṇavī yā trayī mayī ātma sapta gaṇa stham tam bhāsvantam adhitiṣṭhati tayā ca adhiṣṭhitaḥ saḥ api jājvalīti sva raśmibhiḥ tamaḥ samasta jagatām nāśam nayati ca akhilam nṛtyantyaḥ apsarasaḥ yānti tasya ca anu niśācarāḥ vahanti pannagāḥ yakṣaiḥ kriyate abhīṣu saṃgrahaḥ na udetā na astam etā ca kadācid śakti rūpa dhṛk viṣṇuḥ viṣṇoḥ pṛthak tasya gaṇāḥ saptavidhaḥ api ayam chāyā darśana saṃyogam sa tam prāpnoti atha ātmanaḥ evam sā vaiṣṇavī śaktiḥ na eva apaiti tatas dvija pitṛ deva manuṣya ādīn sa sadā āpyāyayan prabhuḥ sūrya raśmi suṣumṇā ayaḥ tarpitaḥ tena candramāḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣemaraiḥ śaśvat pīyate vai sudhā mayaḥ pītam tam dvi kalam somam kṛṣṇa pakṣa kṣaye dvija pibanti pataraḥ teṣām bhāskarāt tarpamam tathā ādatte raśmibhiḥ kṣiti saṃstham rasam raviḥ tam utsṛjati bhūtānām puṣṭi artham sasya vṛddhaye tena prīṇāti aśeṣāṇi bhūtāni bhagavān raviḥ pitṛ deva manuṣya ādīn evam āpyāyayati asau pakṣa tṛptim tu devānām pitṝṇām ca eva māsikīm śaśvat tṛptim ca martyānām maitreya arkaḥ prayacchati iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīya iṃśe ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca vīthi āśrayāṇi ṛkṣāṇi dhruva ādhāreṇa veginā hrāsa vṛddhi kramaḥ tasya raśmīnām savituḥ yathā arkasya iva hi tasya aśvāḥ sakṛt yuktāḥ vahanti te kalpam ekam muni śreṣṭha vārī garbha samudbhavāḥ kṣīṇam pītam suraiḥ somam āpyāyayati dīptimān saṃbhṛtam ca ardha māsena tad soma stham sudhā amṛtam devāḥ maitreya sudhā āhārāḥ yatas amarāḥ trayāstriṃśat sahasrāṇi trayastriṃśat śatāni ca trayastriṃśat tathā devāḥ pibanti kṣaṇadākaram kalā dvayā viśiṣṭaḥ tu praviṣṭaḥ sūrya maṇḍalam amā ākhyā raśmau vasati amāvāsyā tatas smṛtā somam pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcid śiṣṭe kalā ātmake apārāhne pitṛ gaṇa ajaghanyam paryupāsate pibanti dvi kalā ākāram śiṣṭā tasya kalā tu yā sudhā amṛta mayī puṇyā tām indoḥ pitaraḥ mune niḥsṛtan tat amāvāsyām gabhastibhyaḥ sudhā amṛtam māsam tṛptim avāpya agryām pitaraḥ santi nirvṛtāḥ saumyāḥ barhiṣadaḥ ca eva agniṣvāttāḥ ca te tridhā evam devān site pakṣe kṛṣṇapakṣe tathā pitṝn vīrudhaḥ ca amṛta mayaiḥ śītaiḥ ap paramāṇubhiḥ vīrudhā oṣadhi niṣpattyā manuṣya paśu kīṭakān āpyāyayati śītāṃśuḥ prākāśya āhlādanena tu piśaṅgaiḥ turagaiḥ yuktaḥ saḥ aṣṭābhiḥ vāyu vegibhiḥ sa varūthaḥ sa anukarṣaḥ yuktaḥ bhū saṃbhavaiḥ hayaiḥ aṣṭa aśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmān bhaumasya api rathaḥ mahān aṣṭābhiḥ pāṇḍuraiḥ yuktaḥ vājibhiḥ kāñcanorathaḥ tasmin tiṣṭhati varṣa ante rāśau rāśau vṛhaspatiḥ ākāśa sambhavaiḥ aśvaiḥ śabalaiḥ syandanam yutam tam āruhya śanais yāti manda gāmī śanaiścaraḥ svarbhānoḥ turagāḥ hi aṣṭau bhṛṅga ābhāḥ dhūsaram ratham ādityāt niḥsṛtaḥ rāhuḥ somam gacchati parvasu tathā ketu rathasya aśvāḥ api aṣṭau vāta raṃhasaḥ palāla dhūma varṇa ābhāḥ lākṣā rasa nibha aruṇāḥ ete mayā grahāṇām vai tava ākhyātāḥ rathāḥ nava graha ṛkṣa tārā dhiṣṇyāni dhruve baddhāni aśeṣatas yāvāntyaḥ ca eva tārāḥ tā tāvantaḥ vāta raśmayaḥ tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vāta viddhāni sarvaśas śiśumāraḥ tu yaḥ proktaḥ sa dhruvaḥ yatra tiṣṭhati sanniveśam ca tasya api śṛṇuṣva muni sattama yat ahnā kurute pāpam tam dṛṣṭvā niśi mucyate yāvantyaḥ ca eva tārāḥ tāḥ śiśumāra āśritāḥ divi yajñaḥ adharaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ dharmaḥ mūrdhānam āśritaḥ hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ ca āste aśvinau pūrva pādayoḥ śiśraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ tasya mitraḥ apānam samāśritaḥ tārakā śiśumārasya na astam eti catuṣṭayam iti eṣa sanniveśaḥ ayam pṛthivyāḥ jyotiṣām tathā dvīpānām udadhīnām ca parvatānām ca kīrtitaḥ varṣāṇām ca nadīnām ca ye ca teṣu vasanti vai teṣām svarūpam ākhyātam saṃkṣepaḥ śruyatām punar padma ākārā samudbhūtā parvata abdhi ādi saṃyutā jyotīṣi viṣṇuḥ bhuvanāni viṣṇuḥ vanāni viṣṇuḥ girayaḥ diśaḥ ca jñāna sva rūpaḥ bhagavān yatas usā vaśeṣa mūrtiḥ na tu vastu bhūtaḥ tatas hi śaila bdhi dharā ādi bhedān jānīhi vijñāna vijṛmbhitāni yadā tu śuddham nija rūpi sarvam karma kṣaye jñānam apāsta doṣam mahī ghaṭa tvam ghaṭataḥ kapālikā kapālikā cūrṇa rajaḥ tatas aṇuḥ jñānam viśuddham vimalam viśo kam aśeṣa lobha ādi nirasta saṅgam etat tu yat saṃvyavahāra bhūtam tatra api ca uktam bhuvana āśritam te yajñaḥ paśuḥ vahniḥ aśeṣa ṛtvij somaḥ surāḥ svarga mayaḥ ca kāmaḥ iti ādi karma āśrita mārga dṛṣṭam bhūḥ ādi bhogāḥ ca phalāni teṣām iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhagavan samyak ākhyātam yat pṛṣṭaḥ asi mayā kila bhū samudra ādi saritām saṃsthānam sthitiḥ viṣṇu ādhāram yathā ca etat trailokyam samavasthitam parama arthaḥ tu te proktaḥ yathājñānam pradhānataḥ bharataḥ sa mahīpālaḥ sālagrāme avasat kila yoga yuktaḥ samādhāya vāsudeve sadā manaḥ puṇyedeśa prabhāvena dhyāyataḥ ca sadā harim vipra tve ca kṛtam tena yat bhūyas su mahātmanā śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca sālagrāme mahābhāgaḥ bhagavat nyasta mānasaḥ saḥ uvāsa ciram kālam maitreya pṛtivīpatiḥ ahiṃsā ādiṣu aśeṣeṣu guṇeṣu guṇinām varaḥ avāpa paramām kāṣṭhām manasaḥ ca api saṃyame yajñeśa acyuta govinda mādhava ananta keśava kṛṣṇa viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśa vāsudeva namaḥ astu te samidh puṣpa kuśa ādānam cakre deva kriyā kṛte na anyāni cakre karmāṇi niḥsaṅgaḥ yoga tāpasaḥ jagāma saḥ abhiṣeka artham ekadā tu mahā nadīm athā ājagāma tat tīram jalam pātum pipāsitā siṃhasya nādaḥ su mahān sarva prāṇi bhayaṅkaraḥ tatas sā sahasā trāsāt āplutā nimnagā taṭam ati ucca ārohaṇena asyāḥ nadyām garbhaḥ papāta ha tam ūhyamānam vegena vīci mālā pariplutam hariṇīm tām vilokya atha vipannām tṛpa tāpasaḥ mṛga potam samādāya nijam āśramam āgataḥ cakāra anudinam ca asau mṛga potasya vai nṛpaḥ poṣaṇam puṣyamāṇaḥ ca sa tena vavṛdhe mune cacāra āśrama paryante tṛṇāni gahaneṣu saḥ dvaram gatvā ca śārdula trāsāt abhyāyayau punar prātar gatvā ati dūram ca sāyam āyāti atha āśramam āsīt cetaḥ samāsaktam na yayau anyatas dvija vimukta rājya tanayaḥ projjhita aśeṣa bāndhavaḥ kim vṛkaiḥ bhakṣitaḥ vyaghraiḥ kim siṃhena nipātitaḥ cirāyamāṇe niṣkrānte tasya āsīt iti mānasam eṣā vasumatī tasya khura agra kṣata karburā mad bāhum kaṇḍūyana paraḥ hi saḥ kṣemeṇa abhyāgata uraṇyāt api mām sukhayiṣyati kuśāḥ kāśāḥ virājante baṭavaḥ sāma āgāḥ iva samādhi bhaṅgaḥ tasya āsīt tad maya tva ādṛta ātmanaḥ kālena gacchatā saḥ atha kālam cakre mahīpatiḥ pitā iva sa astram putreṇa mṛga potena vīkṣitaḥ mṛgam eva tadā adrākṣīt tyajan prāṇān asau api tatas ca tad kāla kṛtām bhāvanām prāpya tādṛśīm jambūmārge mahā araṇye jātaḥ jātismaraḥ mṛgaḥ vihāya mātaram bhūyas sālagrāmam upāyayaḥ śuṣkaiḥ tṛṇaiḥ tathā parṇaiḥ sa kurvan ātma poṣaṇam tatra ca utsṛṣṭa dehaḥ asau jajñe jātismaraḥ dvijaḥ sat ācāravatām śuddhe yoginām pravare kule ātmanaḥ adhigata jñānaḥ deva ādīni mahā mune na papāṭha guru proktam kṛta upanayanaḥ śrutim na dadarśa ca karmāṇi śāstrāṇi jagṛhe na ca uktaḥ api bahuśas kiñcid jaḍa vākyam abhāṣata tat api a saṃskāra guṇam grāmya vākya ukti saṃśritam saṃmānana parām hānim yoga ṛdhaḥ kurute yatas tasmāt careta vai yogī satām dharmam a dūṣayan ātmānam darśayāmāsa jaḍa unmatta ākṛtim jane bhukte kulmāṣa vāṭī ādi śākam vanyam phalam kaṇān kāritaḥ kṣetra karma ādika danna āhāra poṣitaḥ sama akṣa pīna avayavaḥ jaḍa kārī ca karmaṇi sarva loka upakaraṇam babhūva āhāra cetanaḥ tam tādṛśam a saṃskāram vipra ākṛti viceṣṭitam rātrau tam samalaṅkṛtya vaiśasasya vidhānataḥ adhiṣṭhitam mahākālī jñātvā yogeśvaram tathā tatas khaṅgam samādāya niśitam niśi sā tathā kṣattāram krūra karmāṇam acchinat kaṇṭha mūlataḥ tatas sauvīra rājasya prayātasya mahātmanaḥ tam tādṛśam mahātmānam bhasma channam iva analam sa rājā śibikā ārūḍhaḥ gantum kṛtamatiḥ dvija babhūva ikṣumatī tīre kapila ṛṣeḥ vara āśramam śreyaḥ kim atra saṃsāre duḥkha prāye nṛṇām iti praṣṭum tam mokṣa dharma jñam kapila ākhyam mahā munim uvāha śibikām tasya kṣattuḥ vacana coditaḥ nṛṇām viṣṭi gṛhītānām anyeṣām saḥ api madhya gaḥ gṛhītaḥ viṣṭinā vipraḥ sarva jñāna eka bhājanam jātismarā usau papā asya kṣaya kāmaḥ uvāha tām kurvan matimatām śraṣṭhaḥ tad anye tvaritam yayuḥ vilokya nṛpatiḥ saḥ utha viṣamām śibikā gatim kim etat iti āha samam gamyatām śibikā vahāḥ punar tathā eva śibikam vilokya viṣamām hi saḥ śibikā vāhakāḥ projuḥ ayam yāti iti a satvaram rājā uvāca kim śrintaḥ asi alpam adhvānam tvayā ūḍhā śibikā mama kim āyā sa sahaḥ na tvam pīvān asi nirīkṣyase brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca na aham pīvāḥ na ca eva ūḍhā śibikā bhavataḥ mayā rājā uvāca pratyakṣam dṛśyase pīvān adyā api śibikā tvayi brahmaṇaḥ uvāca pratyakṣam bhavatā bhūpa yat dṛṣṭam mama tat vada balavān abalaḥ ca iti vācyam paścāt viśeṣaṇam tvayā ūḍhā śibikā ca iti tvayi adyā api ca saṃsthitā ūrvoḥ jaṅghā dvaya avasthau tad ādhāram tathā udaram skandha āśritā iyam śibikā mama bhāraḥ utra kim kṛtaḥ śibikāyām sthitam ca idam vapuḥ tvad upalakṣitam karma vaśyāḥ guṇaḥ ca ete sattva ādyāḥ pṛthivīpate avidyā saṃcitam karma tat ca a sa iṣeṣu jantuṣu ātmā śuddha ukṣaraḥ śāntaḥ nirguṇaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ tadā pīvān asi iti ittham kayā yuktyā tvayā īritam bhū pāda jaṅghā kaṭi ūru jaṭhara ādiṣu saṃsthite śibikā iyam yathā skandhe tathā bhāraḥ samaḥ tvayā yadā puṃsaḥ sṛthagbhāvaḥ prākṛtaiḥ kāraṇeḥ nṛpa soḍhavyaḥ tu tad āyāsaḥ katham vā nṛpate mayā yad dravyā śibikā ca iyam tad dravyaḥ bhūta saṃgrahaḥ śrī pāraśaraḥ uvāca saḥ api rājā avatīrya ūvyām tad pādau jagṛhe tvaran rājā uvāca bho bho visṛjya śibikām prasādam kuru me dvijaḥ kathyatām kaḥ bhavān atra jālma rūpa dharaḥ sthitaḥ yaḥ bhavān yat nimittam vā yat āgamana kāraṇam tat sarvam kathyatām vidvan mahyam śuśrūṣave tvayā brahmaṇaḥ uvāca śrūyatām saḥ ham iti etat vaktum bhūpa na śakyate dharma adharmau yatas kasmāt kāraṇam pṛcchate tvayā rājā uvāca brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca anātmani ātma vijñānam śabdaḥ vā bhrānti lakṣaṇaḥ jihvā bravīti aham iti danta uṣṭhau tāluke nṛpa etena aham yatas sarve vāc niṣpādana hetavaḥ piṇḍaḥ pṛthak yatas puṃsaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādi lakṣaṇaḥ tatas ham iti kutra etām saṃjñām rājan karomi aham tvam rājā śibikā ca iyam ime vāhāḥ puras sarāḥ vṛkṣāt dāru tatas ca iyam śibikā tvad adhiṣṭhitā kim vṛkṣa saṃjñā vā asyāḥ syāt dāru saṃjñā atha vā nṛpa vṛkṣa ārūḍhaḥ mahā rājaḥ na ayam vadati te janaḥ na ca dāruṇi sarvaḥ tvām bravīti śibikā gatam śibikā dāru saṃghātaḥ racanā sthiti saṃsthitaḥ anviṣyatām nṛpa śreṣṭha tad bhede śibikā tvayā evam chatra śalākānām pṛthagbhāve vimṛśyatām pumān strī gauḥ ajaḥ vājī kuñjaraḥ vihagaḥ taruḥ deha iṣuloka saṃjñā iyam vijñeyā karma hetuṣu śarīra ākṛti bhedāḥ tu bhūpa ete karma yonayaḥ yat tu na anyām saṃjñām upaiti vai pariṇāma ādi saṃbhūtām tat vastu nṛpa tat ca kim patnyāḥ patiḥ pitā sūnoḥ kim tvam bhūpa vadāmi aham kimu pāda ādikam tvam vā tava etat kim mahīpate pṛthakkaraṇa niṣpādyam śakyate nṛpate katham iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīya iṃse trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca rājā uvāca etat viveka vijñānam yat aśeṣeṣu jantuṣu na aham vahāmi śibikām śivikā na mayi sthitā śarīram anyat asmat tau yonā iyam śibikā dhṛtā guṇa pravṛttyā bhūtānām pravṛttiḥ karma coditā pūrvam eva mahābhāgam kapila ṛṣim aham dvija praṣṭum abhyudyataḥ gatvā śreyaḥ kim tu atra śaṃsa me viṣṇoḥ aṃśaḥ jagat moha nāśāya urvīm upāgataḥ saḥ eva bhagavān nūnam asmākam hita kāmyayā tat mahyam praṇatāya tvam yat śreyaḥ paramam dvijaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca bhūpa pṛcchasi kim śreyaḥ parama artham nu pṛcchasi śreyāṃsi a parama arthāni aśeṣāṇi ca bhūpate karma yajña ātmakam śreyaḥ phalam tad prāpti lakṣaṇam śreyaḥ tasya eva saṃyogaḥ śreyaḥ yaḥ parama ātmanaḥ śreyāṃsi evam anekāni śataśas ya sahasrasaḥ vyayaḥ ca kriyate kasmāt kāma prāpti upalakṣaṇaḥ parama arthaḥ hi kāryāṇi kāraṇānām aśeṣatas rājya ādi prāptiḥ atra uktā parama artha tayā yadi ṛk yajuḥ sāma niṣpādyam yajña karma matam tava parama artha bhūtam tatra api śruyatām gadataḥ mama yat tu niṣpādyate kāryam mṛdā kāraṇa bhūtayā tad kāraṇa anugamanāt jñāyate nṛpa mṛṇmayam evam vināśibhiḥ dravyaiḥ samidh ājya kuśa ādibhiḥ niṣpādyate kriyā yā tu sā bhavitrī vināśinī parama arthaḥ ca prājñauḥ abhyupagamyate dhyānam ca eva ātmanaḥ bhūpu paramārtha artha śabditam parama ātma ātmanoḥ yogaḥ parama arthaḥ iti iṣyate tasmāt śreyāṃsi aśeṣāṇi nṛ vaitāni na saṃśayaḥ parama arthaḥ tu bhūpāla saṃkṣepāt śrūyatām mama ekaḥ vyāpī samaḥ śuddhaḥ nirguṇaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ veṇu randhra prabhedena bhedaḥ ṣaṅja ādi saṃjñitaḥ eka svarūpa bhedaḥ ca brāhma karma āvṛti prajaḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca iti ukte mauninam bhūyas cintayānam mahīpatim pratyuvāca atha vipraḥ usau advaita antargatām kathām brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca śrūyatām nṛpa śārdūla yat gītam ṛbhuṇā purā ṛbhu nāmā abhavat putraḥ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ tasya śiṣyaḥ nidāghaḥ bhūt pulastya tanayaḥ purā prādāt aśeṣa vijñānam sa tasmai parayā mudā apāpta jñāna tantrasya na tasya advaita vāsanā devikāyāḥ taṭe vīranagaram nāma vai puram nidāghaḥ nāma yoga jñaḥ ṛbhu śiṣyaḥ avasat purā jagāma saḥ ṛbhuḥ śiṣyam nidāgham avalokakaḥ prakṣālita aṅghri pāṇim ca kṛtā sana parigrahma uvāca sa dvija śreṣṭhaḥ bhujyatām iti sādaram ṛbhuḥ uvāca nidāghaḥ uvāca saktu yāvaka vāṭyānām apūpānām ca me gṛhe ṛbhuḥ uvāca saṃyāva pāyasa ādīni drapsa phāṇitavanti ca nidāghaḥ uvāca bhakṣya upasādhanam mṛṣṭam tena asya annam prasādhaya brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca iti uktā tena sā patnī mṛṣṭam annam dvijasya yat tam bhuktavantam icchātaḥ mṛṣṭam annam mahā munim nidādhaḥ prāha bhūpāla praśraya avanataḥ sthitaḥ nidāghaḥ uvāca api te mānasam svastham āhāreṇa kṛtam dvija ṛmuḥ uvāca na me kṣudh na abhavat tṛptiḥ kasmāt mām paripṛcchasi bhavati ambhasi ca kṣīṇe nṛṇām tṛṣ api jāyate tatas kṣudh sambhava abhāvāt tṛptiḥ asti eva me sadā pumān sarva gataḥ vyāpī ākāśa vat ayam yatas saḥ aham gantā na ca āgantā na eka deśa niketanaḥ mṛṣṭam na mṛṣṭam api eṣā jijñāsā me kṛtā tava kim vakṣyasi iti tatra api śrūyatām dvijasattama kim asvādu atha vā mṛṣṭam bhuñjataḥ asti dvijottama mṛṣṭam eva yathā mṛṣṭam tat eva udvega kārakam a mṛṣṭam jāyate mṛṣṭam mṛṣṭāt udvijate janaḥ ādi madhya avasāneṣu kim annam ruci kārakam mṛṇmayam hi gṛham yadvat mṛdā liptam sthiram bhavet parthivā uyam tathā dehaḥ pārthivaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ guḍaṃphala ādīni tathā pārthivāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tat etat bhavatā jñātvā mṛṣṭa amṛṣṭa vicāri yat brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya parama artha śritam nṛpa prasīda mad hita arthāya kathyatām yat tvam āgataḥ naṣṭaḥ mohaḥ tava ākarṇya vacāṃsi etāni me dvīja ṛbhuḥ uvāca ṛmuḥ asmi tava ācāryaḥ prajñā dānāya te dvija iha āga yāsyāmi parama arthaḥ tava uditaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca pūjataḥ parayā bhaktyā icchātaḥ prayayau ṛbhuḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīye aṃśe pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca nidāgha jñāna dānāya tat eva nagaram yayau nagarasya bahis saḥ utha nidāgham dadṛśe muniḥ mahī bala parīvāre puram viśati pārthive kṣudh kṣāma kaṇṭham āyāntam araṇyāt sa samidh kuśam dṛṣṭvā nidāgham saḥ ṛbhuḥ upagamya abhivādya ca nidāghaḥ uvāca pravivikṣuḥ puram ramyam tena atra sthīyate mayā ṛbhuḥ uvāca nidāghaḥ uvāca ṛbhuḥ uvāca bhavatā na viśeṣeṇa pṛthak cihna upalakṣaṇau tat kathyatām mahābhāga viśeṣaḥ bhavatā anayoḥ jñātum icchāmi aham kaḥ utra gajaḥ kaḥ vā narādhipaḥ nidāghaḥ uvāca ṛbhuḥ uvāca jānāmi aham yathā brahyan tathā mām avabodhaya brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ sahasā āruhya nidāghaḥ prāha tam ṛbhum śrūyatām kathayāmi eṣa yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi upari aham yathā rājā tvam adhas kuñjaraḥ yathā avabodhāya te brahman dṛṣṭāntaḥ darśitaḥ mayā ṛbhuḥ uvāca brāhmamaḥ uvāca na anyasya advaita saṃskāra saṃskṛtam mānasam tathā ṛbuḥ uvāca tava upadeśa dānāya pūrva śuśruṣaṇa ādṛtaḥ guru snehāt ṛbhuḥ nāma nidāgha samupāgataḥ tat etat upadiṣṭam te saṃkṣepeṇa mahāmate paramārtha sāra bhūtam yat advaitam aśeṣatas brāhmaḥ uvāca evam uktvā yayau vidvān nidāgham saḥ ṛbhuḥ guruḥ sarva bhūtāni abhedena dadṛśe sa tadā ātmanaḥ sita nīlāḥ di bhedena yathā ekam dṛśyate nabhaḥ bhrānta dṛṣṭibhiḥ ātmā api tathā ekaḥ san pṛthak pṛthak śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca iti īritaḥ tena sa rājavarḥ tatyāja bhedam parama artha dṛṣṭiḥ iti śrī viṣṇumadṛdvidṛṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti śri viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe dvitīyaḥ oṃśaḥ samāptaḥ atha śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe viṣṇu citti ātma prakāśa ākhya śrīdharīya vyākhyā dvaya upete tṛtīyaḥ ūṃśaḥ prārabhyate śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥ kathitā gurūṇa asamyak bhū samudra ādi saṃsthitiḥ sūrya ādinām ca saṃsthānam jyotiṣām ca ati vistarāt deva ādīnām tathā sṛṣṭiḥ ṛṣīṇām ca api varṇitā manvantarāṇi aśeṣāṇi śrotum icchāmi anukramāt manvantara adhipān ca eva śaka deva purogamān śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca atīta anāgatāni iha yāni manvantarāṇi vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ manuḥ pūrvam paraḥ svārociṣaḥ tathā uttamaḥ tāmasaḥ ca eva raivataḥ cākṣuṣaḥ tathā ṣaṭ ete manavaḥ utītāḥ sāṃpratam tu raveḥsutaḥ svāyaṃbhuvam tu kathitam kalpa ādau antaram mayā devāḥ saptarṣayaḥ ca eva yathāvat kathitāḥ mayā atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi manoḥ svārociṣasya tu pārāvatāḥ sa tuṣitāḥ devāḥ svārociṣe antare ūrjastaṃbhaḥ tathā pṛṣabhaḥ tathā caitra kiṃpuruṣa ādyāḥ ca sutāḥ svārociṣasya tu dvitīyam etat vyākhyātam antaram śṛṇu ca uttamam suśāntiḥ nāma deva indraḥ maitreya āsīt sutān śṛṇu sudhāmānaḥ tathā satyāḥ japāḥ ca atha pratardanāḥ vaśavartiḥ ca pañca ete gaṇāḥ dvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ ajaḥ paraśudīpta ādyāḥ tathā uttama manoḥ sutāḥ tāmasasya antare devāḥ supārāḥ harayaḥ tathā satyāḥ ca sudhiyaḥ ca eva saptaviṃśatikāḥ gaṇāḥ śiviḥ indraḥ tathā ca āsīt śatayajña upala kṣamaḥ saptarṣa yaḥ ca ye teṣām teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu naraḥ khyātiḥ ketu rūpaḥ jānujaṅgha ādayaḥ tathā putrāḥ tu tāmasasya āsan ājānaḥ su mahā balāḥ manuḥ vibhuḥ ca tatra indraḥ devān ca atra antare śṛṇu amitābhāḥ bhūtarayāḥ vaikuṇṭhāḥ susamedhasaḥ hiraṇya romā veda aśriḥ ūrdhva bāhuḥ tathā avaraḥ vedabāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaḥ ca mahā muniḥ balabandhuḥ ca saṃbhāvyaḥ satyaka ādyāḥ ca tad sutāḥ svārociṣaḥ ca auttamaḥ ca tāmasaḥ raivataḥ tathā priyavrata anvayāḥ hi ete catvāraḥ manavaḥ smṛtāḥ viṣṇum ārādhya tapasā sa rājarṣiḥ priyavrataḥ manvantara adhipān etān laṃbdhavān ātma vaṃśa jān ṣaṣṭhe ca āsīt cākṣuṣa ākhyaḥ tathā manuḥ āpyāḥ prasūtāḥ bhavyāḥ ca divaukasaḥ mahā anubhāvāḥ lakhāḥ ca pañca ete hi aṣṭakāḥ gaṇāḥ sumedhāḥ virajāḥ ca eva haviṣmān uttamaḥ madhuḥ atināmā sahiṣṇuḥ ca sapta āsan iti ca ṛṣayaḥ ūruḥ pūruḥ śatadhyumna pramukhāḥ su mahā balāḥ cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayaḥ abhavan manuḥ saṃvartate dhīmān sāṃpratam saptamentare āditya vasu rudra ādyāḥ devāḥ ca atra mahā mune vaśiṣṭhaḥ kāśyapaḥ uthātriḥ jamadagniḥ sa gautamaḥ ikṣvākuḥ ca nṛgaḥ ca eva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātiḥ eva ca nariṣyantaḥ ca vikhyātaḥ nābhāgoriṣṭaḥ eva ca karūṣaḥ ca pṛṣadhraḥ ca su mahān loka viśrutaḥ manvantareṣu aśeṣeṣu deva tvena adhitiṣṭhati aṃśena tasyāḥ jajñe asau yajñaḥ svāyaṃbhuventare tatas punar sa vai devaḥ prāpte svārociṣa intare tuṣitāyām samutpannaḥ hi ājiṣaḥ tuṣitaiḥ saha raivate api antare devaḥ saṃbhūtyām mānasaḥ hariḥ cākṣuṣe ca antare devaḥ vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ vikuṇṭhāyām asau jajñe vaikuṇṭhaiḥ daivataiḥ saha vāmanaḥ kāśyapāt viṣṇuḥ adityām saṃbabhūva ha tribhiḥ kramaiḥ imān lokān jitvā yena mahātmanā saptasu eva abhavan vipra yābhiḥ saṃvardhitāḥ prajāḥ yasmāt viṣṭam idam viśvam yasya śaktyā mahātmanaḥ tasmāt sa procyate viṣṇuḥ viśoḥ dhātoḥ praveśanāt indraḥ cayaḥ ayam tridaśa īśa bhūtaḥ viṣṇoḥ aśoṣāḥ tu vibhūtayaḥ tāḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhaviṣyāṇi api viprarṣa mama ākhyātum tvam arhasi śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca sūryasya patnī saṃjñā abhūt tanayā viśvakarmaṇaḥ a sahantī tu sā bhartuḥ tejaḥ chāyām yuyoja vai bhartṛ śuśrūṣaṇe araṇyam svayam ca tapase yayau saṃjñā iyam iti atha arkaḥ ca chāyāyām ātmaja trayam śanaiścaram manum ca anyam tapatīm ca api ajājanat chāyā saṃjñā dadau śāpam yamāya kupitā yadā tatas vivasvān ākhyātām tayā eva araṇya saṃsthitām samādhi dṛṣṭyā dadṛśe tām aśvām tapasi sthitām vāji rūpa dharaḥ saḥ utha tasyām devau atha aśvinau āninye ca punar saṃjñām sva sthānam bhagavān raviḥ tejasaḥ śamanam ca asya viśvakarmā cakāra ha kṛtavān aṣṭamam bhāgam sa vyaśātayat avyayam yat tasmāt vaiṣṇavam tejaḥ śātitam viśvakarmaṇā tvaṣṭā eva tejasā tena viṣṇoḥ cakram akalpayat triśūlam ca eva śarvasya śibikām dhanadasya ca śaktim guhasya devānām anyeṣām ca yat āyudham chāyā saṃjñā sutaḥ yaḥ asau dvitīyaḥ kathitaḥ manuḥ tat śṛṇuṣva mahābhāga bhaviṣyat kathayāmi te sutapāḥ ca amitābhāḥ ca mukhyāḥ ca api tathā surāḥ teṣām gaṇāḥ ca devānām ekaikaḥ viṃśakaḥ smṛtaḥ dīptimān gālavaḥ rāmaḥ kṛpaḥ droṇiḥ tathā paraḥ mad putraḥ ca tathā vyāsaḥ ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ ca saptamaḥ viṣṇu prasādāt anaghaḥ pātāla antara gocaraḥ virajāḥ ca urvarīvān ca nirmoka ādyāḥ tathā apare sāvarṇeḥ tu manoḥ putrāḥ bhaviṣyanti nareśvarāḥ pārāḥ marīcigarbhāḥ ca sudharmāṇaḥ tathā tridhā bhaviṣyanti tathā devāḥ hi oka ekaḥ dvādaśaḥ gaṇaḥ pṛthuśrava ādyāḥ ca tathā dakṣamāvarṇika ātmajāḥ sūdhāmānaḥ viśuddhāḥ ca śatasaṃkhyāḥ tathā surāḥ teṣām indraḥ ca bhavitā śāntiḥ nāma mahā balaḥ saptarṣayaḥ bhaviṣyanti ye tathā tān śṛṇuṣva ha haviṣmān sukṛtaḥ satyaḥ tapomūrtiḥ tathā aparaḥ sukṣetraḥ ca uttamaujāḥ ca bhūriṣeṇa ādayaḥ daśa brahmasāvarṇi putrāḥ tu rakṣiṣyanti vasuṃdharām ekādaśaḥ ca bhavitā dharmasāvarṇikaḥ manuḥ vihaṅgamāḥ kāma āgamāḥ nirvāṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā gaṇāḥ tu ete tadā mukhyāḥ devānām ca bhaviṣyatām ā ekaikaḥ triṃśakaḥ teṣām gaṇaḥ ca indraḥ ca vai pṛṣā niḥ svaraḥ ca agnitejāḥ ca vapuṣmān ghaṇiḥ āruṇiḥ haviṣmān anaghaḥ ca eva bhāvyāḥ saptarṣayaḥ tathā sarvatraga sūdharmā ca devānīka ādayaḥ tathā bhaviṣyanti manoḥ tasya tanayāḥ pṛti viśvarāḥ rudraputraḥ tu sāvarṇiḥ bhavitā dvādaśaḥ manuḥ ṛkudhāmā ca tatra idraḥ bhavitā śṛṇu me surān sukarmāṇaḥ surāpāḥ ca daśakāḥ pañca vai gaṇāḥ devavān upadevaḥ ca devaśreṣṭha ādayaḥ tathā manoḥ tasya mahā vīryāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahā nṛpāḥ sutrāmāṇaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sudharmāṇaḥ tathā amarāḥ trayastriṃśat vibhedāḥ āsta devānām yatra vai gaṇāḥ dhṛtimān avyayaḥ ca anyaḥ saptamaḥ sutapāḥ muniḥ śuciḥ indraḥ sura gaṇaḥ tatra pañca śṛṇuṣva tān cākṣuṣāḥ ca pavitrāḥ ca kaniṣṭhāḥ bhrājikāḥ tathā vācavṛddhaḥ ca vai devāḥ saptarṣīn api me śṛṇu agnibāhuḥ śuciḥ śukraḥ māgadhaḥ ugnīdhraḥ eva ca yuktaḥ tathā jitaḥ ca anyaḥ manu putrān atas śṛṇu ūru gaṃbhīra buddhi ādyāḥ manoḥ tasya sutāḥ nṛpāḥ kathitāḥ muni śārdula pālayiṣyanti ye mahīm catur yuga ante vedānām jāyate kila viplavaḥ kṛte kṛte smṛteḥ vipra praṇetā jāyate manuḥ manuḥ saptarṣayaḥ devāḥ bhūpālāḥ ca manoḥ sutāḥ tāvat pramāṇā ca niśā tatas bhavati sattama brahma rūpa dharaḥ śete śeṣa ahau aṃbu saṃplave tatas prabuddhaḥ bhagavān yathā pūrvam tathā punar sṛṣṭim karoti avyaya ātmā kalpe kalpe rajaḥ gumaḥ manavaḥ bhūbhujaḥ sa iṃdrāḥ devāḥ saptarṣayaḥ tathā caduryugā upi asau viṣṇuḥ sthiti vyāpāra lakṣamaḥ kṛte yuge param jñānam kapila ādi sva rūpa dhṛk cakravarti svarūpeṇa tretāyām api sa prabhūḥ vedam ekam catur bhedam kṛtvā śākhā śataiḥ vibhuḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca sarva bhūtāt mahātmanaḥ manvantarāṇi aśeṣāṇi kathitāni mayā tavā iti śri viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ viṣṇuḥ viṣṇo viṣṇutaḥ ca na param vidyate tatas etat tu śrotum icchāmi vyastāḥ vedāḥ mahātmanā bhagavan śāśā bhedān ca me vada śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca veda drumasya maitreya śākhā bhedāḥ sahasraśas na śaktaḥ vistarāt vaktum sa īkṣepeṇa śṛṇuṣva tam dvāpare dvāpare viṣṇuḥ vyāsa rūpī mahā mune vīryam tejaḥ balam ca alpam manuṣyāṇām avekṣya ca hitāya sarva bhūtānām veda bhedān karoti saḥ vedavyāsa abhidhānā tu sā ca mūrtiḥ madhrudviṣaḥ yathā ca bhedaḥ śākhānām vyāsena kriyate mune aṣṭaviṃśati kṛtvas vai vedaḥ vyastaḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ vedavyāsāḥ vyatītāḥ ye hi aṣṭar viśati sattama caturdhā yaiḥ kṛtaḥ vedaḥ dvāpareṣu punar punar tṛtīye ca uśanāḥ vyāsaḥ caturthe ca bṛhaspatiḥ savitā pañcame vyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyuḥ smṛtaḥ prabhuḥ saptame ca tathā eva indraḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṣṭame smṛtaḥ sārasvataḥ ca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ ekādaśe tu triśikhaḥ bharadvājaḥ tatas paraḥ trayodaśe ca āntarikṣaḥ varṇī ca api caturdaśe trayyāruṇaḥ pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe tu dhanañjayaḥ kratuñjayaḥ saptadaśe tad ūrdhvam ca jayaḥ smṛtaḥ atha haryātmanaḥ unte ca smṛtaḥ vājaśravāḥ muniḥ somaśuṣkāyaṇaḥ tasmāt tṛṇabinduḥ iti smṛtaḥ ṛkṣaḥ bhūt bhārgavaḥ tasmāt vālmīkiḥ yaḥ abhidhīyate jātukarṇaḥ bhavat mattaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tatas aṣṭaviṃśatiḥ iti ete vedavyāsāḥ purātanāḥ ekaḥ vedaḥ caturdhā tu taiḥ kṛtaḥ dvāpara ādiṣu bṛha tvāt bṛṃhaṇa tvāt ca tat brahyā iti abhidhīyate praṇava avasthitam nityam bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar iti īryate ṛk yajuḥ sāma atharvāṇaḥ yat tasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ agādha apāram akṣayyam jagat saṃmohana ālayam sva prakāśa pravṛttibhyām puruṣa artha prayojanam saṃkhya jñānavatām niṣṭhā gatiḥ śama dama ātmanām pradhānam ātma yoniḥ ca guhā saṃstham ca śabdyate avibhāgam tathā śukram akṣayam bahudhā ātmakam yat rūpam vāsudevasya paramātma svarūpiṇaḥ saḥ ṛk mayaḥ sāma mayaḥ sarva ātmā sa yajuḥ mayaḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma sāra ātmā saḥ eva ātmā śarīriṇām śākhā praṇetā sa samasta śākhā jñāna svarūpaḥ bhagavān asaṃgaḥ iti kṣiviṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca ādyaḥ vedaḥ catuṣpādaḥ kṛtaḥ sāhasra saṃmitaḥ tat anena eva vedānām śākhā bhedān dvijottama kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam vyāsam viddhi nārāyaṇam prabhum tena vyastāḥ yathā vedāḥ mad putreṇa mahātmanā atha śiṣyān prajagrāha caturaḥ vedapāragān ṛgveda pāṭhakam pailam jagrāha sa mahā muniḥ vaiśaṃpāyana nāmānam yajurvedasya ca agrahīt romaharṣaṇa nāmānam mahā buddhim mahā muniḥ sūtam jagrāha śiṣyam saḥ itihāsa purāṇayoḥ audgātram sāma ābhiḥ cakre brahmatvam ca api atharvabhiḥ tatas saḥ ṛcaḥ uddhṛtya ṛgvedam kṛtavān muniḥ yajṛṃṣi ca yajurvedam sāmavedam ca sāma ābhaḥ rājñām ca atharvavedena sarva karmāṇi ca prabhuḥ caturdhā sa vibheda atha bāṣkalopi ca saṃhitām bodha ādibhyaḥ dadau tāḥ ca śiṣyebhyaḥ sa mahā muniḥ bodhya agni māḍhakau tad ūdyājñavalkya parāśarau pratiśākhāḥ tu śākhāyāḥ tasyāḥ te jagṛhuḥ mune indrapramitiḥ ekām tu saṃhitām sva sūtam tatas māṇḍukeyam mahātmānam maitreya adhyāpayat tadā tasya śiṣya praśiṣyebhyaḥ putra śiṣya kramāt yayau vedamitraḥ tu śākalyaḥ saṃhitām tām adhītavān cakāra saṃhitāḥ pañca śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau ca tāḥ tasya śiṣyāḥ tu ye pañca teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu mudgalaḥ gomakhaḥ ca eva vātsyaḥ śālīyaḥ eva ca śarīraḥ pañcamaḥ ca āsīt maitreya su mahāmatiḥ saṃhitā tritayam cakre śākapūrṇaḥ tathā itaraḥ iti etāḥ pratiśākhābhyaḥ hi anuśākhāḥ dvijottama bāṣkalaḥ ca aparāḥ tistraḥ saṃhitāḥ kṛtavān dvija śiṣyaḥ kālāyaniḥ gārgyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ ca kathājapaḥ iti etāḥ bahvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitāḥ yaiḥ pravartitāḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca yajuḥ vetadaroḥ śākhāḥ saptaviṃśat mahā muniḥ vaiśaṃpāyana nāmāsaḥ vyāsa śiṣyaḥ cakāra vai śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāḥ ca jagṛhuḥ te pi anukramāt śiṣyaḥ parama dharma jñaḥ guru vṛtti paraḥ sadā ṛṣiḥ yaḥ udya mahāmeroḥ samāje nā āgamiṣyati pūrvam evam muni gaṇaiḥ samayaḥ yaḥ kṛtaḥ dvija vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ ekaḥ tu tam vyatikrāntavān tadā sva strīyam bālakam sotha padā spṛṣṭam atāḍayat śiṣyān āha sa bhoḥ śiṣyāḥ brahmahattyā apaham vratam tatas kruddhaḥ guruḥ prāha yājñavalkyam mahā munim mucyatām yat tvayā adhītam mattaḥ vipra avamānaka nistejasaḥ vadasi enā anyat tvam brāhmaṇam puṅgavān tena śiṣyeṇa na arthaḥ usti mama ājñā bhaṅga kāriṇā mama api alam tvayā adhītam yat mayā tat idam dvija śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ rudhira aktāni sa rūpāṇi yajūṃṣi atha visṛṣṭāni yājñavalkyena vai dvija jagṛhuḥ tittirāḥ bhūtvā taittirīyāḥ tu te tatas brahma hattyā vratam cīrṇam guruṇā coditaiḥ tu taiḥ yājñavalkyaḥ upi maitreya prāṇāyāma parāyaṇaḥ tṛṣṭāva prayataḥ sūryam yajūṃṣi abhilaṣan tatas yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca ṛk yajuḥ sāma bhūtāya trayī dhāmne ca te namaḥ namaḥ agnīṣoma bhūtāya jagataḥ kāraṇa ātmane kalā kāṣṭhā nimeṣa ādi kāla jñāna ātma rūpiṇe dhyeyāya viṣṇu rūpāya parama akṣara rūpiṇe bibharti yaḥ sura gaṇān āpyāya indum sva raśmibhiḥ svadhā amṛtena ca pitṝn tasmai tṛpti ātmane namaḥ hima aṃbu gharma vṛṣṭīnām kartā bhartā ca yaḥ prabhuḥ spṛṣṭaḥ yad aṃśubhiḥ lokaḥ kriyā yogyaḥ hi jāyate pavitra kāraṇa ātmāya tasmai śuddha ātmane namaḥ ādityāya ādi bhūtāya deva ādīnām namaḥ namaḥ hiraṇmayam ratham yasya ketavaḥ umṛta vājinaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca vāji rūpa dharaḥ prāha vāñchitam yājñavalkyaḥ tadā prāha praṇipatya divākaram yajūṃṣi tāni me dehi yāni saṃti na me gurau śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca ayātayāma saṃjñāni yāni vetti na tad guruḥ yajūṃṣi yaiḥ adhītāni tāni vipraiḥ dhija uttama vājinaḥ te samākhyātāḥ sūryaḥ api aśvaḥ bhavat yatas śākhā bhedāḥ tu teṣām vai daśa pañca ca vājinām kāṇva ādyāḥ su mahābhāgāḥ yājñavalkyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca sāmaveda taroḥ śākhāḥ vyāsa śiṣyasya jauminiḥ susaṃtuḥ tasya putraḥ bhūt sūtvānaḥ ca abhavat sutaḥ adhītavantau ca ekaikām saṃhitām tau hiraṇyanābhaḥ kausalyaḥ pauṣpiṃjiḥ ca dvijottama udīcyāḥ sāmagāḥ śiṣyāḥ tasya pañcaśatam smṛtāḥ hiraṇyanābhāt tāvatyaḥ saṃhitāḥ yaiḥ dvijottamaiḥ gṛhītāḥ te api ca ucyante paṇḍitaiḥ prācya sāmagāḥ lokākṣiḥ naidhamiḥ ca eva kakṣivān lāṅgaliḥ tathā pauṣpiji śiṣyāḥ tad bhedaiḥ saṃhitāḥ bahulīkṛtāḥ hiraṇyanābha śiṣyaḥ tu caturviśati saṃhitāḥ provāca kṛta nāmā asau śiṣyebhyaḥ ca mahā muniḥ taiḥ ca api sāmavedaḥ asau śākhābhiḥ bahulīkṛtaḥ atharvaṇām atho vakṣye saṃhitānām samuccayam śiṣyam adhyāpayāmāsa kabandham saḥ api tam dvidhā pathyasya api trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ kṛtāḥ yaiḥ dvija saṃhitāḥ jābāliḥ kumudādiḥ ca tṛtīyaḥ śaunakaḥ dvija śaunakaḥ tu dvidhā kṛtvā dadau ekām tu babhrave dvitīyām saṃhitām prādāt saindhavāya yaḥ saṃjñine nakṣatrakalpaḥ vedānām saṃhitānām tathā eva ca caturthaḥ syāt āṅgirasaḥ śāntikalpaḥ ca pañcamaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ tu atharvaṇām ete saṃhitānām vikalpakāḥ ākhyānaiḥ ca api upākhyānaiḥ gāthābhiḥ kalpa śuddhibhiḥ purāṇa saṃhitām cakre purāṇa artha viśāradaḥ prakhyātaḥ vyāsa śiṣyaḥ bhūt sūtaḥ vai romaharṣaṇaḥ purāma saṃhitām tasmai dadau vyāsaḥ mahāmatiḥ sumatiḥ ca agnivarcāḥ ca mitrāyuḥ śāṃsapāyanaḥ akṛtavraṇa sāvarṇiḥ paṣ śiṣyāḥ tasya ca abhavan kāśyapaḥ saṃhitā kartā sāvarṇiḥ śāṃsapāyanaḥ romaharṣāṇikā ca anyā tisṝṇām mūla saṃhitā catuṣṭayena bhedena saṃhitānām idam mune ādyam sarva purāṇānām purāṇam brāhmam ucyate aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni purāṇa jñāḥ pracakṣate brāhmam pādmam vaiṣṇavam ca śaivam bhāgavatam tathā tathā anyam nāradīyam ca mārkaṇḍeyam ca saptamam āgneyam aṣṭamam ca eva bhaviṣyat navamam smṛtam daśamam brahmavaivartam laiṅgam ekādaśam smṛtam vārāham dvādaśam ca eva skāndam ca atra trayodaśam caturdaśam vāmanam ca kaurmam pañcadaśam tathā mātsyam ca gāruḍam ca eva brahmāṇḍam ca tatas param mahā purāṇāni etāni hi aṣṭādaśa mahā mune tathā ca upa purāṇāni munibhiḥ kathitāni ca sargaḥ ca pratisargaḥ ca vaṃśa manvantarāṇi ca sarveṣu eteṣu kathyante vaṃśānucārītam ca yat aṅgāni vedāḥ catvāraḥ mīmāṃsā nyāya vistaraḥ purāṇam dharma śāstram ca vidyāḥ hi etāḥ caturdaśa arthaśāstram caturtham tu hi aṣṭādaśa eva tāḥ jñeyāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ pūrvam tebhyaḥ devarṣayaḥ punar rāja ṛṣayaḥ punar tebhyaḥ ṛṣi prakṛtayaḥ trayaḥ iti śākhāḥ samākhyātaḥ śākhā bhedāḥ tathā eva ca kartāraḥ ca eva śākhānām bheda hetuḥ tathā uditaḥ sarva manvantareṣu evam śākhā bhedāḥ samāḥ smṛtāḥ etat te kathitam sarvam yat pṛṣṭaḥ aham iha tvayā iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśeḥṣṭhaḥ udhyāyaḥ yathā vat kathitam sarvam yat pṛṣṭaḥ asim mayā guro sapta dvīpāni pātāla vidhayaḥ ca mahā mune brahmāṇḍasya asya sarvatas sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ tathā sūkṣma sūkṣma asūkṣmataraiḥ smṛtā sthūlāt sthūlataraiḥ ca eva sarvam prāṇibhiḥ āvṛtam tathā yānti yātanāḥ tad pracoditāḥ yātanābhyaḥ paribhraṣṭāḥ deva ādyāsu atha yoniṣu jantavaḥ parivartante śāstrāṇām eṣa nirṇayaḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ prāha bhīṣmaḥ yat tat śṛṇuṣva me bhīṣṇaḥ uvāca purā mama āgataḥ vatsa sakhā kāliṅgakaḥ dvijaḥ sa mām uvāca praṣṭaḥ vai mayā jātismaraḥ muniḥ sa pṛṣṭaḥ ca mayā bhūyas śraddadhānena vai dvijaḥ prāha kāliṅgakaḥ vipraḥ smṛtvā tasya muneḥ vacaḥ kāliṅgaḥ uvāca sva puruṣam abhivīkṣya pāśa hastam vadati yamaḥ kila tasya karṇa mūle kṣiti tala paramāṇavaḥ nila ante punar upayānti yathā eka tām dharitryāḥ sphaṭika giri śilā amalaḥ kva viṣṇuḥ manasi nṛṇām kva ca matsara ādi doṣaḥ apagata mada māna matsarāṇām tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām hṛdi yadi bhagavān anādiḥ āste hariḥ ari śaṅkha gadā dharaḥ vyātmā harati para dhanam nihanti jantūn vadati tathā yaḥ ca na sahati para saṃpadam vinindām kaluṣa matiḥ kurute satām asādhuḥ śaṭha matiḥ upayāti yaḥ ṛtha tṛṣṇām tam adhama ceṣṭam avehi na asya bhaktam kamala nayana vāsudeva viṣṇo dharaṇidhara acyuta śaṅkha cakra pāṇe kāliṅgaḥ uvāca śrī bhīṣmaḥ uvāca kaliṅga deśāt ādeśya itya prītena su mahātmanā yathā viṣṇu mṛtena anyattrāṇām saṃsāra sāgare kiṅkarāḥ pāśa daṇḍāḥ ca na yamaḥ na ca yātanāḥ samarthāḥ tasya yasya ātmā keśava ālaṃbanaḥ sadā śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhagavan bhagavān devaḥ saṃsāra vijigīṣubhiḥ samākhyāhi jagannāthaḥ viṣṇuḥ ārādhyate yathā ārādhitāt ca govindāt ārādhana paraiḥ naraiḥ śrī parāśaraḥ uvāca aurvaḥ prāha yathā pṛṣṭaḥ tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu viṣṇoḥ ārādhana upāya saṃbandham muni sattama phalam ca ārādhite viṣṇo yat puṃsām abhijāyate sa ca āha pṛṣṭaḥ yatnena tasmai tat mekhilam śṛṇu prāpnoti ārādhite viṣṇau nirvāṇam api ca uttamam yat tu pṛcchasi bhūpāla kathām ārādhyate hariḥ varṇa āśrama ācāravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān viṣṇuḥ ārādhyate panthāḥ na anyaḥ tad toṣa kārakaḥ tasmāt sat ācāravatā puruṣeṇa janārdanaḥ ārādhyaḥ tu sva varṇa ukta dharma anuṣṭhāna kārimā brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śudraḥ ca pṛthivīpate para apavādam paiśunyam anṛtam ca na bhāṣate na tāḍayati no hanti prāṇinaḥ na ca hiṃsakaḥ devāḥ dvija gurūṇām ca śuśrūṣāsu sadā udyataḥ yasya rāga ādi doṣeṇa na duṣṭam nṛpa mānasam varṇa āśrameṣu ye dharmāḥ śāstra uktāḥ muni sattama teṣu tiṣṭhan naraḥ viṣṇum āduṣṭam nṛpa mānasam tat aham śrotum icchami varṇa dharmān aśeṣatas brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām śudrāṇām ca yathākamam tvam ekāgra matiḥ bhūtvā śṛṇu dharmān mayā uditān dānam dadyāt yajet devān yajñiḥ svādhyāya tatparaḥ vṛtti artham yājayet ca anyān anyān adhyāpayet tathā kuryāt pratigraha ādānam śukla arthāt nyāyataḥ dvijaḥ sarva bhūta hitam kuryāt na ahitam kasyācid dvijaḥ ṛtau abhigamaḥ patnyām śastate ca asya pārthiva dānāni dadyāt icchātaḥ dvijebhyaḥ kṣatriyaḥ api vā śastra ājīvaḥ mahī rakṣā pravarā tasya jīvikā dharitrī pālanena eva kṛtakṛtyāḥ narādhipāḥ bhavanti tṛpateḥ aṃśāḥ yatas yajña ādi karmaṇām duṣṭānām śāsanāt rājā śiṣṭānām paripālanāt prāpnoti abhimatān lokān varṇa saṃsthām karoti yaḥ pāśupālyam ca vāṇijyam kṛṣim ca manuja īśvara vaiśyāya jīvikām brahmā dadau lokapitāmahaḥ tasya api adhyayanam yajñaḥ dānam dharmaḥ ca śasyate nitya naimittika ādīnām anuṣṭhānam ca karmaṇām dvijāti saṃśritam karma tādarthyam tena poṣaṇam śudrasya sannatiḥ śaucam sevā svāmini amāyayā dānam ca dadyāt śūdraḥ upi pākayajñaiḥ yajeta ca bhṛtya ādi bharaṇa arthāya sarveṣām ca parigrahaḥ ṛtu kāla abhigamanam sva dāreṣu mahīpate dayā samasta bhūteṣu titikṣā na atimāni tā satyam śaucam anāyāsaḥ maṅgalam priya vādi tā maitrī aspṛhā tathā tadvat akārpaṇyam nareśvara ca sāmānya varṇānām kathitāḥ guṇāḥ āśramāṇām ca sarveṣām ete sāmānya lakṣaṇāḥ guṇān tathāvat dharmān ca vipra ādīnām imān śṛṇu kṣāttram karma dvijasya uktam vaiśyam karma tathā padi dharmān āśramiṇām samyak bruvataḥ me niśāmaya iti śri viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ bālaḥ kṛta upanayanaḥ veda āharaṇa tatparaḥ śaucā ācāra vratam tatra kāryam śuśrūṣaṇam guroḥ ubhe saṃdhye ravim bhūpa tathā eva agnim samāhitaḥ sthite tiṣṭhet vājet yāte nīcais āsīta ca āsati śiṣyaḥ guroḥ nṛpa śreṣṭha pratikūlam na saṃcaret tena e vā uktam paṭhet vedam na anya cittaḥ puras sthitaḥ anujñātaḥ ca bhikṣā annam aśnīyāt guruṇā tatas avagāhet apaḥ pūrvam ācāryeṇa avagāhitaḥ samidh jala ādikam ca asya kālyam kālyam upānayet gṛhīta grāhya vedaḥ ca tatas anujñām avāpya ca gārhasthyam āviśet prājñaḥ niṣpanna guru niṣkṛtiḥ vidhinā avāpta dāraḥ tu dhanam prāpya sva karmaṇā gṛhastha kāryam akhilam kuryāt bhūpāla śaktitaḥ nivāpena pitṝn arcan yajñaiḥ devān tathā atithīn bikṣā bhujaḥ ca ye kecid parivraj brahmacāriṇaḥ veda āharaṇa kāryāya tīrtha snānāya ca prabho aṭanti vasudhām viprāḥ pṛthivī darśanāya ca aniketāḥ hi anāhārāḥ yatra sāyaṅgṛhāḥ ca ye teṣām gṛhasthaḥ sarveṣām pratiṣṭhā yoniḥ eva ca teṣām svāgata dāna ādi vaktavyam madhuram nṛpa gṛha āgatānām dadyāt ca śayana āsana bhojanam sa dattvā duṣkṛtam tasmai puṇyam ādāya gacchati avajñānam ahaṅkāraḥ daṃbhaḥ ca eva sataḥ paritāpa upaghātau ca pāruṣyam ca na śasyate vayaḥ parīṇataḥ rājan kṛtakṛtyaḥ gṛhāśramī putreṣu bhāryām nikṣipya vanam gacchet saha eva vā parṇa mūla phala āhāraḥ keśa śmaśru jaṭā dharaḥ bhūmi śāyī bhavet tatra muniḥ sarva atithiḥ nṛpa carma kāśa kuśaiḥ kuryāt paridhāna uttarīyake tadvat triṣavaṇam snānam śastam asya nareśvaraḥ vanyaḥ trehena gātrāṇām abhyaṅgaḥ ca asya śasyate tapaḥ ca tasya rāja indra śīta uṣṇa ādi sahiṣṇu tā yaḥ tu etām niyataḥ caryām vānaprasthaḥ caret muniḥ sa dahati agni vat doṣān jayet lokān ca śāśvatān caturthaḥ ca āśramaḥ bhikṣoḥ projyate yaḥ manīṣibhiḥ traivargikān tyajet sarvān āraṃbhān avanīpate jarāyu ja aṇḍaja ādīnām vāc manaḥ kāya karmabhiḥ yuktaḥ kurvīta na droham sarva saṃgān ca varjayet tathā tiṣṭhet yathā a prītiḥ dveṣaḥ vā na asya jāyate prāṇayātrā nimittam ca vyaṅgāre bhuktavat jane kāle praśasta varṇānām bhikṣā artham paryaṭet gṛhān kṛtvā agnihotram sva śarīra saṃstham śārīram agnim sva mukhe juhoti mokṣośramam yaḥ carate yathoktam śuciḥ sukham kalpita buddhi yuktaḥ iti śrī viṣṇu mahāpurāṇe tṛtīya aṃśe navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kathitam cāturāśramyam cāturvarṇya kriyāḥ tathā nitya naimittikāḥ kāmyāḥ kriyāḥ puṃsām aśeṣatas samākhyāhi bhṛgu śreṣṭha sarva jñaḥ hi asi me mataḥ tat aham kathayiṣyāṃmi śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ mama jātasya jātakarma ādi kriyā kāṇḍam aśeṣatas putrasya kurvīta pitā śrāddham ca abhyudaya ātmakam yugmān tu prāḍmukhān viprān bhojayet manubha īśvara dadhnā yuktaiḥ sa badaraiḥ miśrān piḍān mudā yutaḥ prājāpatyena vā sarvam upacāram pradakṣiṇam kurvīta tat tathā aśeṣa vṛddhi kāleṣu bhūpate deva pūrvam nara ākhyam hi śarma varma ādi saṃyutam śarma iti brāhyaṇasya uktam varma iti kṣatra saṃśrayam gupta dāsa ātmakam nāma praśastam vaiśya śudrayoḥ na artha hīnam na ca aśastam na apaśabda yutam tathā na amaṅgalyam jugupsākam nāma kuryāt sama akṣaram na ati dīrgham na ati hrasvam na ati guru akṣara anvitam sukha uccāryam tu tat
